   802	
   803	### T10.7b — CREATE OR REPLACE `client_node_place` + `_apply_client_place` med klient-aktiv-check (V7 — Mathias-terminal-V6 #1)
   804	
   805	- **Type:** migration (CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION × 2)
   806	- **Hvad:** Krav-dok §2.5.2 punkt 2 ("Inaktiv klient bliver stående for historik, men kan ikke vælges som ny team-tilknytning") + §3.4 ("valideres at klienten faktisk findes") håndhæves via wrapper og apply-handler. FK fra T10.7 garanterer eksistens, men kun aktiv-check garanterer at deaktiverede klienter ikke kan placeres. Apply-pathen tjekker også fordi pending kan oprettes mens klienten er aktiv og applies efter deaktivering.
   807	- **Designvalg:**
   808	  - **Wrapper-rækkefølge:** `has_permission` → team-only pre-check → klient-eksistens (P0002) → klient-aktiv (22023, **superadmin-bypass via `is_admin()`**) → `pending_change_request`. Eksisterende-check kommer FØR aktiv-check så fejl-meddelelsen er informativ. Team-check kommer FØR klient-check så T9-test T2's `gen_random_uuid` fejler i team-check (uændret 22023-semantik).
   809	  - **Apply-handler-rækkefølge:** payload-validation → team-aktiv-check (uændret fra T9-supplement) → klient-eksistens (P0002) → **employee-baseret admin-tjek** (via `is_admin_by_employee_id(requested_by)` OR `is_admin_by_employee_id(approved_by)`) → klient-aktiv (P0001, bypass hvis admin involveret) → INSERT/UPDATE. **V10 (Codex runde 9):** apply bruger employee-id-baseret check (ikke `auth.uid()`) for at fungere konsistent i cron-context.
   810	  - **Superadmin-bypass-design:** Wrapper kører altid med auth-context → `is_admin()` virker. Apply kører i to contexts: direct admin-call OG cron-apply (`pending_changes_apply_due` job uden auth). For konsistens er apply-bypass baseret på pending-rækkens employee-historie (requested_by + approved_by). "Bypass hvis EITHER er superadmin" matcher "superadmin må alt"-reglen (Mathias 2026-05-21) på tværs af execution-contexts. Eksistens-check (P0002) bypasses IKKE — FK håndhæver alligevel.
   811	  - **`client_node_close` rør IKKE:** Lukning af placement ved klient-deaktivering er legitim forretnings-flow. Aktiv-check her ville blokere det.
   812	- **Eksakt indhold:**
   813	
   814	  ```sql
   815	  -- V10 (Codex runde 9 TEKNISK-BLOKERING): ny helper der tjekker admin-status
   816	  -- via employee_id direkte (ikke auth.uid()). Apply-handler bruger den for
   817	  -- konsistens i cron-apply-context hvor auth.uid() er NULL.
   818	  create or replace function core_identity.is_admin_by_employee_id(p_employee_id uuid)
   819	  returns boolean
   820	  language sql stable security invoker set search_path = ''

exec
/bin/bash -lc "nl -ba docs/coordination/trin-10-plan.md | sed -n '820,1120p'" in /home/mathias/stork-2.0
 succeeded in 0ms:
   820	  language sql stable security invoker set search_path = ''
   821	  as $$
   822	    select exists (
   823	      select 1
   824	      from core_identity.employees e
   825	      join core_identity.role_page_permissions p on p.role_id = e.role_id
   826	      where e.id = p_employee_id
   827	        and core_identity.is_active_employee_state(e.anonymized_at, e.termination_date)
   828	        and p.page_key = 'system'
   829	        and p.tab_key = 'manage'
   830	        and p.scope = 'all'
   831	        and p.can_edit = true
   832	    );
   833	  $$;
   834	  comment on function core_identity.is_admin_by_employee_id(uuid) is
   835	    'V10/Trin 10: admin-tjek via employee_id (ikke auth.uid). Anvendes af apply-handlers der kører i cron-context uden auth.';
   836	  -- Grant-pattern matcher is_admin() (T1-helpers-stubs:50): authenticated + anon + service_role.
   837	  -- Service_role-grant er for cron-vejen (pending_changes_apply_due-job uden auth-context).
   838	  revoke all on function core_identity.is_admin_by_employee_id(uuid) from public;
   839	  grant execute on function core_identity.is_admin_by_employee_id(uuid) to authenticated, anon, service_role;
   840	
   841	  -- Wrapper: tilføj klient-aktiv-check efter team-check
   842	  create or replace function core_identity.client_node_place(
   843	    p_client_id uuid,
   844	    p_node_id uuid,
   845	    p_effective_from date
   846	  ) returns uuid language plpgsql security definer set search_path = ''
   847	  as $$
   848	  declare
   849	    v_request_id uuid;
   850	    v_client_active boolean;
   851	  begin
   852	    if not core_identity.has_permission('client_placements', 'manage', true) then
   853	      raise exception 'permission_denied' using errcode = '42501';
   854	    end if;
   855	    -- Pre-check: node_id skal være team (uændret fra T9).
   856	    if not exists (
   857	      select 1 from core_identity.org_node_versions
   858	      where node_id = p_node_id and node_type = 'team' and is_active = true
   859	        and effective_from <= current_date
   860	        and (effective_to is null or effective_to > current_date)
   861	    ) then
   862	      raise exception 'client_placement_node_not_team_or_inactive: %', p_node_id using errcode = '22023';
   863	    end if;
   864	    -- V7/Trin 10 (krav-dok §3.4 + §2.5.2): klient skal findes og være aktiv.
   865	    select is_active into v_client_active
   866	      from core_identity.clients where id = p_client_id;
   867	    if not found then
   868	      raise exception 'client_not_found: %', p_client_id using errcode = 'P0002';
   869	    end if;
   870	    if v_client_active = false and not core_identity.is_admin() then
   871	      raise exception 'client_inactive: % er sat is_active=false (krav-dok §2.5.2: inaktiv klient kan ikke vælges som ny team-tilknytning)', p_client_id
   872	        using errcode = '22023';
   873	    end if;
   874	    -- V9 (Codex runde 8 TEKNISK-BLOKERING): pending_changes-INSERT-policy
   875	    -- (T9-fundament-supplement) kræver session-var. T9-public-wrapper sætter
   876	    -- den ikke (latent bug); trin 10 lukker for client-RPC'erne.
   877	    perform set_config('stork.t9_write_authorized', 'true', true);
   878	    v_request_id := core_identity.pending_change_request(
   879	      'client_place', p_client_id,
   880	      jsonb_build_object(
   881	        'client_id', p_client_id::text,
   882	        'node_id', p_node_id::text,
   883	        'effective_from', p_effective_from::text
   884	      ),
   885	      p_effective_from
   886	    );
   887	    return v_request_id;
   888	  end; $$;
   889	
   890	  revoke execute on function core_identity.client_node_place(uuid, uuid, date) from public, anon;
   891	
   892	  -- V9 (Codex runde 8 TEKNISK-BLOKERING): client_node_close får også t9_write_authorized.
   893	  -- INGEN aktiv-check (krav-dok §2.5.2 gælder ikke for lukning; deaktivering skal kunne
   894	  -- lukke placement).
   895	  create or replace function core_identity.client_node_close(
   896	    p_client_id uuid,
   897	    p_effective_from date
   898	  ) returns uuid language plpgsql security definer set search_path = ''
   899	  as $$
   900	  declare v_request_id uuid;
   901	  begin
   902	    if not core_identity.has_permission('client_placements', 'manage', true) then
   903	      raise exception 'permission_denied' using errcode = '42501';
   904	    end if;
   905	    -- V9: pending_changes-INSERT-policy kræver session-var.
   906	    perform set_config('stork.t9_write_authorized', 'true', true);
   907	    v_request_id := core_identity.pending_change_request(
   908	      'client_close', p_client_id,
   909	      jsonb_build_object(
   910	        'client_id', p_client_id::text,
   911	        'effective_from', p_effective_from::text
   912	      ),
   913	      p_effective_from
   914	    );
   915	    return v_request_id;
   916	  end; $$;
   917	
   918	  revoke execute on function core_identity.client_node_close(uuid, date) from public, anon;
   919	
   920	  -- Apply-handler: tilføj klient-eksistens + aktiv-check FØR INSERT/UPDATE
   921	  create or replace function core_identity._apply_client_place(
   922	    p_payload jsonb,
   923	    p_pending_change_id uuid
   924	  ) returns void
   925	  language plpgsql security definer set search_path = ''
   926	  as $$
   927	  declare
   928	    v_client_id uuid;
   929	    v_node_id uuid;
   930	    v_effective_from date;
   931	    v_client_active boolean;
   932	    v_active record;
   933	    v_requested_by uuid;
   934	    v_approved_by uuid;
   935	    v_admin_involved boolean;
   936	  begin
   937	    v_client_id := (p_payload->>'client_id')::uuid;
   938	    v_node_id := (p_payload->>'node_id')::uuid;
   939	    v_effective_from := (p_payload->>'effective_from')::date;
   940	    if v_client_id is null or v_node_id is null or v_effective_from is null then
   941	      raise exception 'invalid_payload: client_id + node_id + effective_from required'
   942	        using errcode = '22023';
   943	    end if;
   944	
   945	    -- Team-aktiv-check (uændret fra T9-supplement).
   946	    if not exists (
   947	      select 1 from core_identity.org_node_versions
   948	      where node_id = v_node_id and node_type = 'team' and is_active = true
   949	        and effective_from <= v_effective_from
   950	        and (effective_to is null or effective_to > v_effective_from)
   951	    ) then
   952	      raise exception 'client_placement_requires_active_team: %', v_node_id
   953	        using errcode = 'P0001';
   954	    end if;
   955	
   956	    -- V7/Trin 10 (krav-dok §3.4 + §2.5.2): klient skal findes og være aktiv.
   957	    -- Fanger pending oprettet mens aktiv, applied efter deaktivering.
   958	    select is_active into v_client_active
   959	      from core_identity.clients where id = v_client_id;
   960	    if not found then
   961	      raise exception 'apply_client_place: client_not_found: %', v_client_id using errcode = 'P0002';
   962	    end if;
   963	
   964	    -- V10 (Codex runde 9 TEKNISK-BLOKERING): bypass kan IKKE bruge is_admin()
   965	    -- fordi auth.uid() er NULL i cron-apply-context. Hent requester+approver fra
   966	    -- pending-rækken og tjek via employee-id-baseret helper.
   967	    v_admin_involved := false;
   968	    if p_pending_change_id is not null then
   969	      select requested_by, approved_by into v_requested_by, v_approved_by
   970	        from core_identity.pending_changes where id = p_pending_change_id;
   971	      v_admin_involved :=
   972	        core_identity.is_admin_by_employee_id(v_requested_by) or
   973	        (v_approved_by is not null and core_identity.is_admin_by_employee_id(v_approved_by));
   974	    end if;
   975	
   976	    if v_client_active = false and not v_admin_involved then
   977	      raise exception 'apply_client_place: client_inactive: % (krav-dok §2.5.2)', v_client_id
   978	        using errcode = 'P0001';
   979	    end if;
   980	
   981	    -- Resten af apply-handler-logikken er uændret fra T9-supplement
   982	    -- (20260520000000_t9_supplement.sql:321-350): find aktiv placement,
   983	    -- enten INSERT ny, UPDATE eksisterende eller split placement-række.
   984	    select * into v_active
   985	    from core_identity.client_node_placements
   986	    where client_id = v_client_id
   987	      and effective_from <= v_effective_from
   988	      and (effective_to is null or effective_to > v_effective_from)
   989	    limit 1;
   990	
   991	    if not found then
   992	      insert into core_identity.client_node_placements
   993	        (client_id, node_id, effective_from, effective_to, created_by_pending_change_id)
   994	      select v_client_id, v_node_id, v_effective_from,
   995	        (select min(effective_from) from core_identity.client_node_placements
   996	         where client_id = v_client_id and effective_from > v_effective_from),
   997	        p_pending_change_id;
   998	    elsif v_active.effective_from = v_effective_from then
   999	      update core_identity.client_node_placements
  1000	      set node_id = v_node_id,
  1001	          created_by_pending_change_id = coalesce(p_pending_change_id, created_by_pending_change_id),
  1002	          updated_at = now()
  1003	      where id = v_active.id;
  1004	    else
  1005	      update core_identity.client_node_placements
  1006	      set effective_to = v_effective_from, updated_at = now()
  1007	      where id = v_active.id;
  1008	      insert into core_identity.client_node_placements
  1009	        (client_id, node_id, effective_from, effective_to, created_by_pending_change_id)
  1010	      values
  1011	        (v_client_id, v_node_id, v_effective_from, v_active.effective_to, p_pending_change_id);
  1012	    end if;
  1013	  end; $$;
  1014	
  1015	  revoke execute on function core_identity._apply_client_place(jsonb, uuid) from public, anon, authenticated;
  1016	  ```
  1017	
  1018	- **Impact-analyse for eksisterende T9-tests:**
  1019	  - `t9_placements.sql` T5 + T7 + T9 (med fixture-seedede klienter fra T10.7a, default `is_active=true`): aktiv-check passerer. ✓
  1020	  - `t9_placements.sql` T6 (`_apply_client_place` på department + `gen_random_uuid`-klient): team-check fejler først → uændret semantik.
  1021	  - `t9_backdated_historical_traversal.sql` BLOCK 3: fixture-klienter er aktive. ✓
  1022	  - `t9_public_wrapper_rpcs.sql` T2 (`gen_random_uuid` + department): team-check fejler først → uændret 22023. ✓
  1023	- **Afhængigheder:** T10.1 (clients-tabel + is_active-kolonne), T10.7 (FK)
  1024	- **Migration-fil:** `supabase/migrations/<ts>_t10_client_active_check.sql`
  1025	- **Risiko:** lav. Rollback: CREATE OR REPLACE med T9-supplements oprindelige definitioner.
  1026	
  1027	### T10.8 — `client_upsert` RPC (uden logo-parametre)
  1028	
  1029	- **Type:** migration (CREATE FUNCTION)
  1030	- **Hvad:** SECURITY DEFINER write-RPC for clients. has_permission-baseret. Logo-felter rør'es IKKE her (separate RPC'er i T10.11 forhindrer datatab).
  1031	- **Eksakt indhold:**
  1032	
  1033	  ```sql
  1034	  create or replace function core_identity.client_upsert(
  1035	    p_name text,
  1036	    p_fields jsonb,
  1037	    p_change_reason text,
  1038	    p_is_active boolean default true,
  1039	    p_client_id uuid default null
  1040	  ) returns uuid
  1041	  language plpgsql security definer set search_path = ''
  1042	  as $$
  1043	  declare
  1044	    v_id uuid;
  1045	  begin
  1046	    if not core_identity.has_permission('clients', 'manage', true) then
  1047	      raise exception 'client_upsert: permission_denied' using errcode = '42501';
  1048	    end if;
  1049	    if p_change_reason is null or length(trim(p_change_reason)) = 0 then
  1050	      raise exception 'client_upsert: change_reason er paakraevet' using errcode = '22023';
  1051	    end if;
  1052	    if p_name is null or length(trim(p_name)) = 0 then
  1053	      raise exception 'client_upsert: name er paakraevet' using errcode = '22023';
  1054	    end if;
  1055	
  1056	    perform set_config('stork.source_type', 'manual', true);
  1057	    perform set_config('stork.change_reason', p_change_reason, true);
  1058	    perform set_config('stork.allow_clients_write', 'true', true);
  1059	
  1060	    if p_client_id is null then
  1061	      -- INSERT: p_is_active anvendes (default true for nye klienter)
  1062	      insert into core_identity.clients (name, fields, is_active)
  1063	      values (p_name, coalesce(p_fields, '{}'::jsonb), p_is_active)
  1064	      returning id into v_id;
  1065	    else
  1066	      -- V8 (Code walk-through #2): UPDATE rør IKKE is_active (default true ville reaktivere
  1067	      -- inaktiv klient utilsigtet ved ren navne-ændring). Brug client_set_active for toggle.
  1068	      -- Matcher logo-pattern (rør'es heller ikke i client_upsert).
  1069	      update core_identity.clients
  1070	        set name = p_name,
  1071	            fields = coalesce(p_fields, '{}'::jsonb)
  1072	            -- is_active rør IKKE (brug client_set_active)
  1073	            -- logo-felter rør IKKE (brug client_logo_set/clear)
  1074	       where id = p_client_id
  1075	       returning id into v_id;
  1076	      if v_id is null then
  1077	        raise exception 'client_upsert: client % findes ikke', p_client_id using errcode = 'P0002';
  1078	      end if;
  1079	    end if;
  1080	
  1081	    return v_id;
  1082	  end;
  1083	  $$;
  1084	
  1085	  revoke all on function core_identity.client_upsert(text, jsonb, text, boolean, uuid) from public, anon;
  1086	  grant execute on function core_identity.client_upsert(text, jsonb, text, boolean, uuid) to authenticated;
  1087	  ```
  1088	
  1089	- **Afhængigheder:** T10.1, T10.13 (permission-row seeded)
  1090	- **Migration-fil:** `supabase/migrations/<ts>_t10_client_upsert_rpc.sql`
  1091	- **Risiko:** lav.
  1092

  1136	### T10.10 — `client_field_definition_upsert` RPC (uden p_match_role; V3: immutable key + pii_level-downgrade-block)
  1137	
  1138	- **Type:** migration (CREATE FUNCTION)
  1139	- **Hvad:** SECURITY DEFINER write-RPC for client_field_definitions. has_permission('client_field_definitions', 'manage', true). **V3 (Codex V2 KRITISK-SIKKERHEDSHUL):** UPDATE forbyder ændring af `key` (audit-PII-hash i clients.fields ville miste reference); UPDATE forbyder pii_level direct → non-direct (eksisterende værdier ville pludselig skrives i klartekst i audit). For at ændre `key`: marker den gamle definition `is_active=false` og INSERT en ny. For at sænke pii-niveau: behandl som ny definition.
  1140	- **Eksakt indhold:**
  1141	
  1142	  ```sql
  1143	  create or replace function core_identity.client_field_definition_upsert(
  1144	    p_key text,
  1145	    p_display_name text,
  1146	    p_field_type text,
  1147	    p_pii_level text,
  1148	    p_change_reason text,
  1149	    p_required boolean default false,
  1150	    p_display_order integer default 0,
  1151	    p_is_active boolean default true,
  1152	    p_field_id uuid default null
  1153	  ) returns uuid
  1154	  language plpgsql security definer set search_path = ''
  1155	  as $$
  1156	  declare
  1157	    v_id uuid;
  1158	    v_existing_key text;
  1159	    v_existing_pii text;
  1160	  begin
  1161	    if not core_identity.has_permission('client_field_definitions', 'manage', true) then
  1162	      raise exception 'client_field_definition_upsert: permission_denied' using errcode = '42501';
  1163	    end if;
  1164	    if p_change_reason is null or length(trim(p_change_reason)) = 0 then
  1165	      raise exception 'client_field_definition_upsert: change_reason er paakraevet' using errcode = '22023';
  1166	    end if;
  1167	    if p_pii_level not in ('none', 'indirect', 'direct') then
  1168	      raise exception 'client_field_definition_upsert: pii_level skal vaere none/indirect/direct' using errcode = '22023';
  1169	    end if;
  1170	
  1171	    perform set_config('stork.source_type', 'manual', true);
  1172	    perform set_config('stork.change_reason', p_change_reason, true);
  1173	    perform set_config('stork.allow_client_field_definitions_write', 'true', true);
  1174	
  1175	    if p_field_id is null then
  1176	      insert into core_identity.client_field_definitions
  1177	        (key, display_name, field_type, required, pii_level, display_order, is_active)
  1178	      values
  1179	        (p_key, p_display_name, p_field_type, p_required, p_pii_level, p_display_order, p_is_active)
  1180	      returning id into v_id;
  1181	    else
  1182	      -- V3 (Codex V2 KRITISK-SIKKERHEDSHUL): forbyd key-rename og direct → non-direct
  1183	      -- for eksisterende definitions. Audit-PII-hashing i clients.fields stoler på at
  1184	      -- key+pii_level er stabile for værdier der allerede ligger i jsonb.
  1185	      select key, pii_level into v_existing_key, v_existing_pii
  1186	        from core_identity.client_field_definitions
  1187	       where id = p_field_id;
  1188	      if not found then
  1189	        raise exception 'client_field_definition_upsert: field % findes ikke', p_field_id using errcode = 'P0002';
  1190	      end if;
  1191	      if v_existing_key is distinct from p_key then
  1192	        raise exception 'client_field_definition_upsert: key er immutable (% -> %). For at omdøbe: marker eksisterende felt is_active=false og INSERT et nyt.', v_existing_key, p_key
  1193	          using errcode = '22023', hint = 'Audit-PII-hash i clients.fields binder til key.';
  1194	      end if;
  1195	      if v_existing_pii = 'direct' and p_pii_level <> 'direct' then
  1196	        raise exception 'client_field_definition_upsert: pii_level direct -> % afvist. Eksisterende vaerdier i clients.fields ville pludselig skrives i klartekst i audit-log.', p_pii_level
  1197	          using errcode = '22023', hint = 'For at saenke pii-niveau: INSERT ny definition med ny key.';
  1198	      end if;
  1199	
  1200	      -- V8 (Code walk-through #3): UPDATE rør IKKE is_active (default true ville reaktivere
  1201	      -- inaktiv felt-definition utilsigtet ved ren navne-ændring). Brug client_field_definition_set_active.
  1202	      update core_identity.client_field_definitions
  1203	        set display_name = p_display_name,
  1204	            field_type = p_field_type,
  1205	            required = p_required,
  1206	            pii_level = p_pii_level,
  1207	            display_order = p_display_order
  1208	            -- key rør'es ikke (verificeret immutable ovenfor)
  1209	            -- is_active rør IKKE (brug client_field_definition_set_active)
  1210	       where id = p_field_id
  1211	       returning id into v_id;
  1212	    end if;
  1213	
  1214	    return v_id;
  1215	  end;
  1216	  $$;
  1217	
  1218	  revoke all on function core_identity.client_field_definition_upsert(text, text, text, text, text, boolean, integer, boolean, uuid) from public, anon;
  1219	  grant execute on function core_identity.client_field_definition_upsert(text, text, text, text, text, boolean, integer, boolean, uuid) to authenticated;
  1220	  ```
  1221	
  1222	  **Semantik (V3):** `key` er funktionelt immutable efter INSERT — audit-PII-hash i `clients.fields` binder til key. `pii_level` kan eskaleres (none → indirect → direct) men ikke downgrades fra direct (eksisterende klartekst-værdier ville opstå i audit). For at ændre key eller sænke pii-niveau: deaktiver eksisterende definition + INSERT ny.
  1223	
  1224	- **Afhængigheder:** T10.2, T10.13
  1225	- **Migration-fil:** `supabase/migrations/<ts>_t10_client_field_definition_upsert_rpc.sql`
  1226	- **Risiko:** lav.
  1227	
  1228	### T10.10a — `client_field_definition_set_active` RPC (V8 — Code walk-through #4; krav-dok §3.2)
  1229	
  1230	- **Type:** migration (CREATE FUNCTION)
  1231	- **Hvad:** Toggler `is_active` på felt-definition uden at røre øvrige felter. Matcher `client_set_active`-mønstret (T10.9) + krav-dok §3.2's "Deaktivér felt-definition" som distinct funktion. Adskilt RPC fordi UI-flowet er distinkt (knap "deaktiver felt" vs. "redigér felt").
  1232	- **Eksakt indhold:**
  1233	
  1234	  ```sql
  1235	  create or replace function core_identity.client_field_definition_set_active(
  1236	    p_field_id uuid,
  1237	    p_is_active boolean,
  1238	    p_change_reason text
  1239	  ) returns void
  1240	  language plpgsql security definer set search_path = ''
  1241	  as $$
  1242	  begin
  1243	    if not core_identity.has_permission('client_field_definitions', 'manage', true) then
  1244	      raise exception 'client_field_definition_set_active: permission_denied' using errcode = '42501';
  1245	    end if;
  1246	    if p_change_reason is null or length(trim(p_change_reason)) = 0 then
  1247	      raise exception 'client_field_definition_set_active: change_reason er paakraevet' using errcode = '22023';
  1248	    end if;
  1249	
  1250	    perform set_config('stork.source_type', 'manual', true);
  1251	    perform set_config('stork.change_reason', p_change_reason, true);
  1252	    perform set_config('stork.allow_client_field_definitions_write', 'true', true);
  1253	
  1254	    update core_identity.client_field_definitions
  1255	      set is_active = p_is_active
  1256	     where id = p_field_id;
  1257	    if not found then
  1258	      raise exception 'client_field_definition_set_active: field % findes ikke', p_field_id using errcode = 'P0002';
  1259	    end if;
  1260	  end;
  1261	  $$;
  1262	
  1263	  revoke all on function core_identity.client_field_definition_set_active(uuid, boolean, text) from public, anon;
  1264	  grant execute on function core_identity.client_field_definition_set_active(uuid, boolean, text) to authenticated;
  1265	  ```
  1266	
  1267	- **Afhængigheder:** T10.2, T10.13
  1268	- **Migration-fil:** samme som T10.10 eller separat
  1269	- **Risiko:** lav.

  1271	### T10.11 — Logo-RPC'er (`client_logo_set` + `client_logo_clear` + `client_logo_get`)
  1272	
  1273	- **Type:** migration (CREATE FUNCTION × 3)
  1274	- **Hvad:** Dedikerede RPC'er for logo. Set kræver alle tre felter ikke-NULL (matcher T10.1's consistency-CHECK). Clear nulstiller alle tre atomisk. Get returnerer bytea + metadata.
  1275	- **Eksakt indhold:**
  1276	
  1277	  ```sql
  1278	  create or replace function core_identity.client_logo_set(
  1279	    p_client_id uuid,
  1280	    p_logo_bytes bytea,
  1281	    p_logo_content_type text,
  1282	    p_logo_filename text,
  1283	    p_change_reason text
  1284	  ) returns void
  1285	  language plpgsql security definer set search_path = ''
  1286	  as $$
  1287	  begin
  1288	    if not core_identity.has_permission('clients', 'manage', true) then
  1289	      raise exception 'client_logo_set: permission_denied' using errcode = '42501';
  1290	    end if;
  1291	    if p_change_reason is null or length(trim(p_change_reason)) = 0 then
  1292	      raise exception 'client_logo_set: change_reason er paakraevet' using errcode = '22023';
  1293	    end if;
  1294	    if p_logo_bytes is null or p_logo_content_type is null or p_logo_filename is null then
  1295	      raise exception 'client_logo_set: alle tre logo-felter er paakraevede (brug client_logo_clear for at fjerne)' using errcode = '22023';
  1296	    end if;
  1297	
  1298	    perform set_config('stork.source_type', 'manual', true);
  1299	    perform set_config('stork.change_reason', p_change_reason, true);
  1300	    perform set_config('stork.allow_clients_write', 'true', true);
  1301	
  1302	    update core_identity.clients
  1303	      set logo_bytes = p_logo_bytes,
  1304	          logo_content_type = p_logo_content_type,
  1305	          logo_filename = p_logo_filename
  1306	     where id = p_client_id;
  1307	    if not found then
  1308	      raise exception 'client_logo_set: client % findes ikke', p_client_id using errcode = 'P0002';
  1309	    end if;
  1310	  end;
  1311	  $$;
  1312	
  1313	  create or replace function core_identity.client_logo_clear(
  1314	    p_client_id uuid,
  1315	    p_change_reason text
  1316	  ) returns void
  1317	  language plpgsql security definer set search_path = ''
  1318	  as $$
  1319	  begin
  1320	    if not core_identity.has_permission('clients', 'manage', true) then
  1321	      raise exception 'client_logo_clear: permission_denied' using errcode = '42501';
  1322	    end if;
  1323	    if p_change_reason is null or length(trim(p_change_reason)) = 0 then
  1324	      raise exception 'client_logo_clear: change_reason er paakraevet' using errcode = '22023';
  1325	    end if;
  1326	
  1327	    perform set_config('stork.source_type', 'manual', true);
  1328	    perform set_config('stork.change_reason', p_change_reason, true);
  1329	    perform set_config('stork.allow_clients_write', 'true', true);
  1330	
  1331	    update core_identity.clients
  1332	      set logo_bytes = null,
  1333	          logo_content_type = null,
  1334	          logo_filename = null
  1335	     where id = p_client_id;
  1336	    if not found then
  1337	      raise exception 'client_logo_clear: client % findes ikke', p_client_id using errcode = 'P0002';
  1338	    end if;
  1339	  end;
  1340	  $$;
  1341	
  1342	  create or replace function core_identity.client_logo_get(p_client_id uuid)
  1343	  returns table (logo_bytes bytea, logo_content_type text, logo_filename text)
  1344	  language plpgsql stable security invoker set search_path = ''
  1345	  as $$
  1346	  begin
  1347	    if not core_identity.has_permission('clients', 'manage', false) then
  1348	      raise exception 'client_logo_get: permission_denied' using errcode = '42501';
  1349	    end if;
  1350	    return query
  1351	      select c.logo_bytes, c.logo_content_type, c.logo_filename
  1352	        from core_identity.clients c
  1353	       where c.id = p_client_id and c.logo_bytes is not null;
  1354	  end; $$;
  1355	
  1356	  revoke all on function core_identity.client_logo_set(uuid, bytea, text, text, text) from public, anon;
  1357	  revoke all on function core_identity.client_logo_clear(uuid, text) from public, anon;
  1358	  revoke all on function core_identity.client_logo_get(uuid) from public, anon;
  1359	  grant execute on function core_identity.client_logo_set(uuid, bytea, text, text, text) to authenticated;
  1360	  grant execute on function core_identity.client_logo_clear(uuid, text) to authenticated;
  1361	  grant execute on function core_identity.client_logo_get(uuid) to authenticated;
  1362	  ```
  1363	
  1364	- **Afhængigheder:** T10.1 (logo-kolonner + consistency-CHECK), T10.13

  1368	### T10.12 — Read-RPC'er (`client_get`, `client_list`, `client_field_definitions_list`)
  1369	
  1370	- **Type:** migration (CREATE FUNCTION × 3)
  1371	- **Hvad:** SECURITY INVOKER read-RPC'er bag has_permission. Returnerer non-logo-felter (logo via dedikeret get).
  1372	- **Eksakt indhold:**
  1373	
  1374	  ```sql
  1375	  create or replace function core_identity.client_get(p_client_id uuid)
  1376	  returns table (
  1377	    id uuid,
  1378	    name text,
  1379	    fields jsonb,
  1380	    is_active boolean,
  1381	    logo_content_type text,
  1382	    logo_filename text,
  1383	    has_logo boolean,
  1384	    created_at timestamptz,
  1385	    updated_at timestamptz
  1386	  ) language plpgsql stable security invoker set search_path = ''
  1387	  as $$
  1388	  begin
  1389	    if not core_identity.has_permission('clients', 'manage', false) then
  1390	      raise exception 'client_get: permission_denied' using errcode = '42501';
  1391	    end if;
  1392	    return query
  1393	      select c.id, c.name, c.fields, c.is_active,
  1394	             c.logo_content_type, c.logo_filename,
  1395	             c.logo_bytes is not null,
  1396	             c.created_at, c.updated_at
  1397	        from core_identity.clients c
  1398	       where c.id = p_client_id;
  1399	  end; $$;
  1400	
  1401	  create or replace function core_identity.client_list()
  1402	  returns table (
  1403	    id uuid, name text, is_active boolean,
  1404	    has_logo boolean, created_at timestamptz, updated_at timestamptz
  1405	  ) language plpgsql stable security invoker set search_path = ''
  1406	  as $$
  1407	  begin
  1408	    if not core_identity.has_permission('clients', 'manage', false) then
  1409	      raise exception 'client_list: permission_denied' using errcode = '42501';
  1410	    end if;
  1411	    return query
  1412	      select c.id, c.name, c.is_active, c.logo_bytes is not null,
  1413	             c.created_at, c.updated_at
  1414	        from core_identity.clients c
  1415	       order by c.name asc;
  1416	  end; $$;
  1417	
  1418	  create or replace function core_identity.client_field_definitions_list(p_include_inactive boolean default false)
  1419	  returns setof core_identity.client_field_definitions
  1420	  language plpgsql stable security invoker set search_path = ''

  1444	### T10.13 — Seed permissions i grant-modellen
  1445	
  1446	- **Type:** migration (INSERT i permission_pages + permission_tabs + role_permission_grants)
  1447	- **Hvad:** Tilføj `clients` + `client_field_definitions` pages under `org_structure`-area; manage-tab pr. page; superadmin grants.
  1448	- **Eksakt indhold:**
  1449	
  1450	  ```sql
  1451	  select set_config('stork.source_type', 'migration', false);
  1452	  select set_config('stork.change_reason',
  1453	    'T10.13: seed permissions for trin 10 RPCs i grant-modellen', false);
  1454	  -- V4 (Codex V3 KRITISK): T9-supplement's INSERT-policies på permission_pages
  1455	  -- / permission_tabs / role_permission_grants kræver stork.t9_write_authorized.
  1456	  select set_config('stork.t9_write_authorized', 'true', false);
  1457	
  1458	  -- 1. Pages under org_structure-area
  1459	  with org_area as (
  1460	    select id from core_identity.permission_areas where name = 'org_structure'
  1461	  )
  1462	  insert into core_identity.permission_pages (area_id, name)
  1463	  select org_area.id, page_name
  1464	  from org_area, (values ('clients'), ('client_field_definitions')) as p(page_name)
  1465	  on conflict (area_id, name) do nothing;
  1466	
  1467	  -- 2. Tabs: 'manage' for hver ny page (V9: scope til org_structure-area for robusthed)
  1468	  insert into core_identity.permission_tabs (page_id, name)
  1469	  select p.id, 'manage'
  1470	  from core_identity.permission_pages p
  1471	  join core_identity.permission_areas a on a.id = p.area_id
  1472	  where p.name in ('clients', 'client_field_definitions')
  1473	    and a.name = 'org_structure'
  1474	  on conflict (page_id, name) do nothing;
  1475	
  1476	  -- 3. Superadmin grants på tab-niveau (V9: scope til org_structure-area for robusthed)
  1477	  insert into core_identity.role_permission_grants
  1478	    (role_id, area_id, page_id, tab_id, can_access, can_write, visibility)
  1479	  select
  1480	    (select id from core_identity.roles where name = 'superadmin'),
  1481	    null, null, t.id,
  1482	    true, true, 'all'
  1483	  from core_identity.permission_tabs t
  1484	  join core_identity.permission_pages p on p.id = t.page_id
  1485	  join core_identity.permission_areas a on a.id = p.area_id
  1486	  where p.name in ('clients', 'client_field_definitions')
  1487	    and a.name = 'org_structure'
  1488	    and t.name = 'manage'
  1489	  on conflict (role_id, coalesce(area_id::text, ''),
  1490	              coalesce(page_id::text, ''), coalesce(tab_id::text, ''))
  1491	  do nothing;
  1492	  ```
  1493	
  1494	- **Afhængigheder:** T9 migration 9 (grant-modellen + `org_structure`-area), T9 (`superadmin`-rolle)
  1495	- **Migration-fil:** `supabase/migrations/<ts>_t10_seed_permissions.sql`
  1496	- **Risiko:** lav (idempotent ON CONFLICT). Rollback: DELETE i omvendt rækkefølge.
  1497	
  1498	### T10.14 — Master-plan-rettelser (jf. krav-dok §7)
  1499	
  1500	- **Type:** docs-ændring (i samme PR som migrations)
  1501	- **Hvad:** Ret §1.8 + §4 trin 10 så match-rolle / crm_match_id / migration-leverance fjernes. Tilføj is_active + logo. Tilføj rettelse-entry i Appendix C.
  1502	- **Konkrete tekst-ændringer (skitse):**
  1503	  - §1.8 erstattes med: "Klient er driftens grundenhed. Stor variation i felter pr. klient — derfor felt-bag, ikke felt-eksplosion. Klient lever i core_identity.clients (id, name, fields jsonb, is_active, logo). Klient-felt-definitions-registry globalt: key, display-navn, type, required, pii-niveau, display-rækkefølge, is_active. Validerings-trigger advarer ved ukendte jsonb-keys (LENIENT-default; strict-mode via session-var). Audit-PII-filter har special-case for jsonb felt-bag: walker keys og hasher hver med pii_level='direct'. Klient anonymiseres ikke; livscyklus = aktiv/inaktiv. Match-mekanik udskudt til data-indgang-pakke."
  1504	  - §4 trin 10-række: erstat hele cellen med: "Klient-skabelon (core_identity.clients + client_field_definitions + logo + is_active + FK fra client_node_placements + has_permission-RPCs)". Migration-tekst og crm_match_id-tekst fjernes.
  1505	  - Appendix C: tilføj rettelse-entry 2026-05-20 med kort beskrivelse + reference til mathias-afgoerelser "Trin 10 scope-præcisering" og denne plan.
  1506	- **Afhængigheder:** ingen — committes parallelt med migrations
  1507	- **Migration-fil:** N/A (docs)
  1508	- **Risiko:** lav. Rollback: git revert.

T3 (apply-path-scenarie): non-admin opretter pending mens klient aktiv → non-admin approver → deaktiver klient → apply → forvent **P0001 `apply_client_place: client_inactive`**. Test SKAL være `begin;` + `rollback;`-wrapped. |

  1547	  ```
  1548	
  1549	- **G-nummer-kandidat:** FK-coverage-fitness-check ikke implementeret per master-plan §3 punkt 19. Registreres som teknisk gæld for senere pakke der implementerer check'en. T9-migration `20260518000004:5` har forhåndsdokumentation der ikke matcher nuværende fitness-script-tilstand.
  1550	- **Afhængigheder:** T10.12 (`client_field_definitions_list`-RPC skal eksistere så allowlist-entry refererer reel funktion)
  1551	- **Risiko:** lav.
  1552	
  1553	---
  1554	
  1555	## Fundament-tjek-passeret
  1556	
  1557	| Tjek                                                           | Status | Reference                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
  1558	| -------------------------------------------------------------- | ------ | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
  1559	| Hver write-RPC har GRANT + INSERT/UPDATE-policy + session-var  | ja     | T10.8/T10.9/T10.10/T10.10a/T10.11 — `stork.allow_clients_write` / `allow_client_field_definitions_write` + `revoke/grant execute` + has_permission('manage', true). **T10.7b** (`client_node_place` + `client_node_close` + `_apply_client_place`) — `stork.t9_write_authorized = 'true'` før `pending_change_request` (V9-fix); apply-handler tjekker eksistens (P0002) + aktiv (P0001) med employee-id-baseret admin-bypass (V10-fix); pending_change_apply-dispatcher (T9-supplement) cases `client_place` + `client_close` ramt automatisk. **T10.13** (permission-seed) — `stork.t9_write_authorized` (V4-fix) som krævet af T9-supplement's INSERT-policies på permission_pages/tabs/role_permission_grants. Default-privileges på `core_identity` schema (T1: `grant execute on functions to authenticated`) dækker GRANT for alle T10-RPC'er. |
  1560	| Hver SELECT-policy bred nok til legitime læsere                | ja     | T10.1, T10.2 — has_permission('clients'/'client_field_definitions', 'manage', false) **tab-aware (V6-fix)**. T10.13 seeder kun tab-grants → null-tab matcher ikke; 'manage' matcher. T9-supplement's ACL-scoped policy på client_node_placements bevares uændret.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
  1561	| Eksempel-row verificeret gennem flow                           | ja     | T10.15 smoke-tests dækker INSERT + UPDATE + read-RPC + permission-spærring + audit-PII-hashing + logo-preserve + FK + LENIENT/strict + immutable-key + pii-downgrade-block + active-check (wrapper + apply-path + cron-context). **T10.7b apply-dispatch:** pending_change_apply (T9-fundament-supplement) dispatcher cases `client_place` + `client_close` rammer modificeret `_apply_client_place` + uændret `_apply_client_close`. **jsonb payload producer/consumer:** wrapper bygger payload via `jsonb_build_object(...)` (producer), apply-handler læser via `(p_payload->>'client_id')::uuid` etc. (consumer) — pattern matcher T9-supplement linje 88-102 + 295-301.                                                                                                                                                                         |
  1562	| Plan-detaljer eksplicit (ingen TBD / Code afgør / overladelse) | ja     | Alle 16 steps har eksakt SQL/pseudo-SQL. Ingen "kan tilføjes senere"-noter.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
  1563

  1584	
  1585	## Build-fase halt-håndtering
  1586	
  1587	- **Forventede WORKAROUND-kandidater:** ingen forventet.
  1588	- **Forventede PLAN-AFVIGELSE-scenarier:**
  1589	  - Hvis T1-audit_filter_values' STABLE-modifier blokerer mig fra at læse client_field_definitions (immutability-issue), kan jeg ende med at skifte til VOLATILE — PLAN-AFVIGELSE med G-nummer-forslag.
  1590	  - Hvis et T9-test bruger client_id i et flow jeg ikke har spottet i recon → PLAN-AFVIGELSE med STOP og recon-først-gentag.
  1591	  - Hvis pnpm fitness rammer andre exemption-entries der ikke findes i recon → markeres som PLAN-AFVIGELSE.
  1592	- **Kritiske invarianter der ikke må brydes:**
  1593	  - FORCE ROW LEVEL SECURITY bevares på alle nye tabeller
  1594	  - audit-trigger-dækning på alle write-tabeller
  1595	  - clients_validate_fields-trigger med LENIENT-default + strict-via-session-var
  1596	  - audit_filter_values' clients-special-case (jsonb-walking for direct-PII keys)
  1597	  - change_reason-disciplin (`stork.change_reason` påkrævet ved alle writes)
  1598	  - has_permission-checks ER write-gate (ikke kun policy-fallback)
  1599	  - T9-supplement's `client_node_placements_select` policy uændret
  1600	
  1601	---
  1602	
  1603	## Optimerings-hypoteser (V5.3 — valgfri)
  1604	
  1605	- **Hypotese 1:** Logo-MIME-validering kunne håndhæves som CHECK constraint på `logo_content_type` (`IN ('image/png', 'image/jpeg', 'image/svg+xml')`) frem for app-niveau. Codex kan rejse som OPTIMERING-FORSLAG.
  1606	- **Hypotese 2:** `client_list` kunne tilbyde valgfri filter på is_active (p_include_inactive default false). Codex kan rejse som ADOPT i build.
  1607	- **Hypotese 3:** `core_compliance.audit_filter_values`'s clients-special-case kan ekstraheres til en generel "jsonb-walking via field-definition-tabel"-mekanik for fremtidige jsonb-felter. Ikke implementeret nu (premature abstraction).
  1608	- **Hypotese 4 (V6 erstatter Codex V1 #4):** T10.4 har nu `on conflict do nothing` (V6 — Mathias-terminal fund #2). Tidligere DEFER-til-G-nummer var forkert: fitness-check `migration-on-conflict-discipline` håndhæver det, ikke optional.
  1609	- **G-nummer-kandidat (Code-validering fund #4):** FK-coverage-fitness-check ikke implementeret per master-plan §3 punkt 19. T9-migration har forhåndsdokumentation der ikke matcher nuværende fitness-script.
  1610	
  1611	---
  1612	
  1613	## Risiko + kompensation
  1614	
  1615	| Migration                               | Værste-case                                                         | Sandsynlighed                                                                          | Rollback                    |
  1616	| --------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | --------------------------- |
  1617	| T10.1 (CREATE clients-tabel)            | Audit-trigger fejler pga. manglende klassifikation                  | lav (T10.4 seedede klassifikation i samme PR; audit_filter_values har LENIENT-default) | drop table cascade          |
  1618	| T10.2 (CREATE client_field_definitions) | Samme som T10.1                                                     | lav                                                                                    | drop table cascade          |
  1619	| T10.3 (allowlist-udvidelse)             | Allowlist-format ændret af senere migration                         | lav (D1b-format stabilt)                                                               | re-create D1b's signatur    |
  1620	| T10.4 (klassifikation INSERT)           | validate_permanent_classification fejler hvis T10.3 ikke kørt først | lav (afhængighed eksplicit)                                                            | DELETE matching rows        |
  1621	| T10.5 (omskriv audit_filter_values)     | Eksisterende audit-flow brækker                                     | mellem (omskriver kerne-funktion)                                                      | re-create T1's signatur     |
  1622	| T10.6 (clients_validate_fields trigger) | Trigger blokerer legitime writes                                    | lav (LENIENT-default)                                                                  | drop trigger + function     |
  1623	| T10.7 (FK)                              | T9-tests brækker                                                    | lav efter T10.7a                                                                       | drop constraint             |
  1624	| T10.7a (test-fixture-seed)              | Side-effekt i andre T9-tests                                        | lav (kun ekstra INSERT)                                                                | git revert                  |
  1625	| T10.8-T10.12 (RPC'er)                   | Signatur-konflikt med tidligere version                             | lav (greenfield; ingen tidligere RPC i core_identity-schema)                           | drop function               |
  1626	| T10.13 (permission-seed)                | INSERT fejler pga. manglende area/role                              | lav (T9-migration 9 har seedede); ON CONFLICT idempotent                               | DELETE i omvendt rækkefølge |
  1627	| T10.14 (master-plan-rettelser)          | Tekst-rettelse rammer Appendix C-tabel forkert                      | lav                                                                                    | git revert                  |
  1628	| T10.15 (smoke-tests)                    | Test rammer flow jeg ikke har spottet                               | lav (recon-først dækkede T9-test-mønster)                                              | revert test-fil             |
  1629	| T10.16 (fitness-script)                 | Allowlist-entry-formatet er ikke som forventet                      | lav (verificeres ved build; STOP hvis afvigelse)                                       | revert script-ændring       |
  1630	
  1631	**Kompensation generelt:** Hver migration er separat fil. Rækkefølge: tabeller (T10.1, T10.2) → klassifikation-grundlag (T10.3, T10.4) → audit/validate (T10.5, T10.6) → FK med test-fix (T10.7a → T10.7) → RPC'er (T10.8-T10.12) → permission-seed (T10.13) → docs + tests + fitness (T10.14-T10.16). Hver checkpoint kan testes isoleret.

  1679	
  1680	## Konklusion
  1681	
  1682	V13 bringer trin 10 i mål: klient-skabelonen etableres greenfield i `core_identity` med aktiv/inaktiv-livscyklus + logo (med PII-hashed audit) + FK fra T9's klient-til-team-tilknytning + permission-baserede write-RPC'er + aktiv-check ved nye team-tilknytninger (krav-dok §2.5.2) + session-var fix på T9-public-wrappers for client + employee-id-baseret admin-bypass i cron-context + komplet fundament-tjek-dækning + apply-vej-test-setup. Klient-tabel eksisterer ikke på main før denne pakke (T1 droppede D5's pre-fundament); 16 steps + 3 sub-steps (T10.7a, T10.7b, T10.10a) skaber alle artefakter fra bunden.
  1683	
  1684	19 leverancer, alle med eksakt SQL/pseudo-SQL. Risiko lav-mellem på alle migrations, hver rollbar individuelt.
  1685	
  1686	V13-ændringer ift. V12 (Codex runde 12):
  1687	
  1688	- T10.15 `t10_client_active_check.sql`: setup-disciplin tilføjet — UPDATE `undo_settings.undo_period_seconds = 0` for `client_place`/`client_close` transaction-local. Omgår T9's 24-timers default-undo-periode der ellers ville få apply til at fejle med `not_yet_due` før aktiv-check rammes. ROLLBACK isolerer.
  1689	
  1690	V12-ændringer ift. V11 (Codex runde 11):
  1691	
  1692	- T10.4: `clients.logo_filename` + `clients.logo_bytes` skiftet til `pii_level='direct'` (audit hasher). `logo_content_type` forbliver `'none'`. Codex KRITISK-SIKKERHEDSHUL: brugerleveret filnavn kunne lande i klartekst i audit_log.
  1693	- T10.15 logo-test: assert at `audit_log.new_values.logo_filename` + `logo_bytes` er SHA256-hashed efter `client_logo_set`.
  1694	
  1695	V11-ændringer ift. V10 (Codex runde 10):
  1696	
  1697	- Fundament-tjek-tabel udvidet med T10.7b's komplette write-vej (`client_node_place` + `client_node_close` + `_apply_client_place` + apply-dispatch + jsonb producer/consumer) + T10.10a (`client_field_definition_set_active`).
  1698	- G058 registreret i teknisk-gaeld.md (FK-coverage-fitness-check ikke implementeret per master-plan §3.19). Oprydnings-strategi-tabel opdateret til "ja" på teknisk-gaeld med G057 + G058.
  1699	
  1700	V10-ændringer ift. V9 (Codex runde 9):
  1701	
  1702	- T10.7b udvidet med ny helper `core_identity.is_admin_by_employee_id(p_employee_id uuid)` — admin-tjek via employee-id (ikke `auth.uid()`).
  1703	- `_apply_client_place` henter `requested_by` + `approved_by` fra pending-rækken og bypasser aktiv-check hvis EITHER er superadmin (Codex runde 9 TEKNISK-BLOKERING).
  1704	- Wrapper `client_node_place` beholder `is_admin()` (auth-context er garanteret).
  1705	- T10.15 smoke-test udvidet med 3 nye cron-context-scenarier (T6 + T7 + T8) der dækker requester-bypass, approver-bypass og no-admin-failure.
  1706	
  1707	V9-ændringer ift. V8 (Codex runde 8):
  1708	
  1709	- T10.7b udvidet: `client_node_place` + ny CREATE OR REPLACE af `client_node_close` sætter `stork.t9_write_authorized = 'true'` før `pending_change_request`. T9-fundament-supplement's `pending_changes_insert`-policy kræver session-var (Codex runde 8 TEKNISK-BLOKERING).
  1710	- T10.13 robusthed: tab/grant-INSERT-queries scope'es til `org_structure`-area via JOIN på area_id (Codex G-NUMMER → ADOPT).
  1711	- Walk-through-disciplin V9: hver T10-RPC's write-vej spores til ALLE berørte RLS-tabeller, ikke kun direkte tabel.
  1712	
  1713	V8-ændringer ift. V7 (Codex runde 7 + Code grundig walk-through "fuldt gear"):
  1714	
  1715	- T10.16 udvidet: `core_identity.clients_validate_fields` tilføjet til `LEGACY_IS_ACTIVE_EXEMPT_FUNCTIONS` (Codex runde 7 KRITISK).
  1716	- T10.8 `client_upsert` UPDATE: `is_active` fjernet fra SET-klausul. p_is_active anvendes kun ved INSERT. Toggle via client_set_active. Forhindrer utilsigtet reaktivering (Code walk-through #2).
  1717	- T10.10 `client_field_definition_upsert` UPDATE: `is_active` fjernet fra SET-klausul (Code walk-through #3).
  1718	- **Ny T10.10a:** `client_field_definition_set_active(p_field_id, p_is_active, p_change_reason)` RPC matcher krav-dok §3.2 "Deaktivér felt-definition" + client_set_active-mønstret (Code walk-through #4).
  1719	- T10.15 udvidet: lifecycle-test assert client_upsert UPDATE bevarer is_active; field-defs-test assert UPDATE bevarer is_active + set_active toggler uafhængigt.
  1720	- Superadmin-bypass: bevares på T10.7b (forretnings-invariant). **IKKE** udvidet til T10.10's key/pii_level-immutable (sikkerheds-invariant, Mathias-bekræftet).
  1721	
  1722	V7-ændringer ift. V6 (Mathias-terminal-review V6 + 2026-05-21 superadmin-rettelse):
  1723	
  1724	- **Ny T10.7b:** CREATE OR REPLACE `client_node_place` + `_apply_client_place` med klient-aktiv-check og **superadmin-bypass**. Krav-dok §2.5.2 håndhæves i både wrapper og apply-path (apply fanger pending oprettet mens aktiv, applied efter deaktivering).
  1725	- T10.15: ny smoke-test `t10_client_active_check.sql` (5 scenarier inkl. superadmin-bypass).
  1726	- Stale-fixes: linje 113 (Verificerede afhængigheder) + linje 142 (Scope) opdateret til at matche T10.16's R7d-allowlist-retning. Linje 68 (V1-fund-tabel) + linje 1335 (Konklusion-historik) markeret som "V6 OVERSKRIVER".
  1727	- T10.4 + Konklusion: "9 kolonner" på `client_field_definitions` rettet til "10 kolonner" (SQL var korrekt; tekst-fejl).
  1728	
  1729	V6-ændringer ift. V5 (Mathias-terminal-review + Code grundig validering):
  1730	
  1731	- T10.1 + T10.2: tilføjet `-- no-dedup-key: <reason>` markers — fitness-check `dedup-key-or-opt-out` blokerer ellers (Mathias #1).
  1732	- T10.4: tilføjet `on conflict (table_schema, table_name, column_name) do nothing` — `core_compliance.data_field_definitions` er på `BOOTSTRAP_CONFIG_TABLES`; tidligere DEFER-til-G-nummer var forkert (Mathias #2).
  1733	- T10.1 + T10.2 SELECT-policies + T10.11 client_logo_get + T10.12 read-RPC'er: alle skiftet fra `has_permission(p, null, false)` til `has_permission(p, 'manage', false)` — tab-aware. T10.13 seeder kun tab-grants så null-tab matcher ikke (Mathias #3).
  1734	- T10.15 `t10_client_node_placements_fk.sql`: eksplicit `begin;` + `rollback;` wrap — `client_node_placements` på `TX_WRAP_REQUIRED_FOR_TEST_INSERT` (Code-validering #6).
  1735	- T10.16 omformuleret: `FK_COVERAGE_EXEMPTIONS` findes ikke i nuværende fitness-script (master-plan §3.19 ikke implementeret); plan tilføjer i stedet `core_identity.client_field_definitions_list` til `LEGACY_IS_ACTIVE_EXEMPT_FUNCTIONS` (Code-validering #4 + #5). G-nummer for FK-coverage-check.
  1736	
  1737	V5-ændring ift. V4 (Codex runde 4 ACCEPT):
  1738	
  1739	- T10.1 + T10.2: tilføjet `grant insert, update on table ... to authenticated` — RLS-policy + session-var kan ikke virke før DML-GRANT er på plads. Ingen DELETE-grant (inaktivering via is_active).
  1740	
  1741	V4-ændring ift. V3 (Codex runde 3 ACCEPT):
  1742

  1744	- Fundament-tjek-tabel udvidet med T10.13's session-var-disciplin.
  1745	
  1746	V3-ændringer ift. V2 (Codex runde 2 ACCEPT på begge fund):
  1747	
  1748	- T10.3: baseret på P1a's komplette VALUES-blok (15 entries inkl. `anonymization_strategies`) + 2 trin 10-entries = 17 total. V2's D1b-baseline var regression (Codex V2 KRITISK #2).
  1749	- T10.10: `key` er funktionelt immutable for eksisterende definitions (UPDATE blokeres). `pii_level` direct → non-direct afvises. Forhindrer audit-PII-datalæk via key-rename eller pii-downgrade (Codex V2 KRITISK-SIKKERHEDSHUL #1).
  1750	- T10.15 smoke-test udvidet med immutable-key + pii-downgrade-block assertions.
  1751	
  1752	V2-ændringer ift. V1 (Codex runde 1 ACCEPT på 3 fund + DEFER på 1):
  1753	
  1754	- T10.1: tilføjet `CHECK (jsonb_typeof(fields) = 'object')` — forhindrer scalar/array i fields-kolonnen (Codex KRITISK #1)
  1755	- T10.5: fjernet `is_active = true`-filter fra audit_filter_values clients-special-case — alle direct-PII keys hashes uanset is_active for at undgå datalæk ved felt-deaktivering (Codex KRITISK-SIKKERHEDSHUL #2)
  1756	- T10.15: smoke-test for non-object fields-reject + audit-PII-hashing efter is_active=false (Codex MELLEM #3 + V2-supplement til #2)
  1757	- T10.4 ON CONFLICT: DEFER → G-nummer (greenfield-engangsmigration). **V6 OVERSKRIVER: ACCEPT** — fitness håndhæver, ON CONFLICT er nu obligatorisk i T10.4.
  1758	
  1759	Hovedlinjer ift. tidligere fabrikerede V1-V3 (`claude/trin-10-plan-v2`-branchen):
  1760	
  1761	- Plan baseret på CREATE TABLE fra bunden (ikke ALTER på droppet D5)
  1762	- Klienter i `core_identity` (ikke `public`)
  1763	- Klassifikation i `core_compliance.data_field_definitions` (ikke `public`)

  1765	- is_permanent_allowed udvides med de to nye tabeller
  1766	- Logo-håndtering i separate RPC'er (forhindrer datatab via client_upsert)
  1767	- T9-supplement-policy uændret
  1768	- Grant-modellen seedes (ikke legacy role_page_permissions)

  1770

  1603	## Optimerings-hypoteser (V5.3 — valgfri)
  1604	
  1605	- **Hypotese 1:** Logo-MIME-validering kunne håndhæves som CHECK constraint på `logo_content_type` (`IN ('image/png', 'image/jpeg', 'image/svg+xml')`) frem for app-niveau. Codex kan rejse som OPTIMERING-FORSLAG.
  1606	- **Hypotese 2:** `client_list` kunne tilbyde valgfri filter på is_active (p_include_inactive default false). Codex kan rejse som ADOPT i build.
  1607	- **Hypotese 3:** `core_compliance.audit_filter_values`'s clients-special-case kan ekstraheres til en generel "jsonb-walking via field-definition-tabel"-mekanik for fremtidige jsonb-felter. Ikke implementeret nu (premature abstraction).
  1608	- **Hypotese 4 (V6 erstatter Codex V1 #4):** T10.4 har nu `on conflict do nothing` (V6 — Mathias-terminal fund #2). Tidligere DEFER-til-G-nummer var forkert: fitness-check `migration-on-conflict-discipline` håndhæver det, ikke optional.
  1609	- **G-nummer-kandidat (Code-validering fund #4):** FK-coverage-fitness-check ikke implementeret per master-plan §3 punkt 19. T9-migration har forhåndsdokumentation der ikke matcher nuværende fitness-script.

  1613	## Risiko + kompensation
  1614	
  1615	| Migration                               | Værste-case                                                         | Sandsynlighed                                                                          | Rollback                    |
  1616	| --------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | --------------------------- |
  1617	| T10.1 (CREATE clients-tabel)            | Audit-trigger fejler pga. manglende klassifikation                  | lav (T10.4 seedede klassifikation i samme PR; audit_filter_values har LENIENT-default) | drop table cascade          |
  1618	| T10.2 (CREATE client_field_definitions) | Samme som T10.1                                                     | lav                                                                                    | drop table cascade          |
  1619	| T10.3 (allowlist-udvidelse)             | Allowlist-format ændret af senere migration                         | lav (D1b-format stabilt)                                                               | re-create D1b's signatur    |
  1620	| T10.4 (klassifikation INSERT)           | validate_permanent_classification fejler hvis T10.3 ikke kørt først | lav (afhængighed eksplicit)                                                            | DELETE matching rows        |
  1621	| T10.5 (omskriv audit_filter_values)     | Eksisterende audit-flow brækker                                     | mellem (omskriver kerne-funktion)                                                      | re-create T1's signatur     |
  1622	| T10.6 (clients_validate_fields trigger) | Trigger blokerer legitime writes                                    | lav (LENIENT-default)                                                                  | drop trigger + function     |
  1623	| T10.7 (FK)                              | T9-tests brækker                                                    | lav efter T10.7a                                                                       | drop constraint             |
  1624	| T10.7a (test-fixture-seed)              | Side-effekt i andre T9-tests                                        | lav (kun ekstra INSERT)                                                                | git revert                  |
  1625	| T10.8-T10.12 (RPC'er)                   | Signatur-konflikt med tidligere version                             | lav (greenfield; ingen tidligere RPC i core_identity-schema)                           | drop function               |
  1626	| T10.13 (permission-seed)                | INSERT fejler pga. manglende area/role                              | lav (T9-migration 9 har seedede); ON CONFLICT idempotent                               | DELETE i omvendt rækkefølge |
  1627	| T10.14 (master-plan-rettelser)          | Tekst-rettelse rammer Appendix C-tabel forkert                      | lav                                                                                    | git revert                  |
  1628	| T10.15 (smoke-tests)                    | Test rammer flow jeg ikke har spottet                               | lav (recon-først dækkede T9-test-mønster)                                              | revert test-fil             |
  1629	| T10.16 (fitness-script)                 | Allowlist-entry-formatet er ikke som forventet                      | lav (verificeres ved build; STOP hvis afvigelse)                                       | revert script-ændring       |
  1630	
  1631	**Kompensation generelt:** Hver migration er separat fil. Rækkefølge: tabeller (T10.1, T10.2) → klassifikation-grundlag (T10.3, T10.4) → audit/validate (T10.5, T10.6) → FK med test-fix (T10.7a → T10.7) → RPC'er (T10.8-T10.12) → permission-seed (T10.13) → docs + tests + fitness (T10.14-T10.16). Hver checkpoint kan testes isoleret.

     6	-- ─── role_permission_grants ─────────────────────────────────────────────
     7	-- no-dedup-key: konfig-tabel; unique index på (role_id, area/page/tab) er natural key.
     8	create table core_identity.role_permission_grants (
     9	  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
    10	  role_id uuid not null references core_identity.roles(id) on delete cascade,
    11	  area_id uuid references core_identity.permission_areas(id) on delete cascade,
    12	  page_id uuid references core_identity.permission_pages(id) on delete cascade,
    13	  tab_id uuid references core_identity.permission_tabs(id) on delete cascade,
    14	  can_access boolean not null default false,
    15	  can_write boolean not null default false,
    16	  visibility text not null default 'self' check (visibility in ('self', 'subtree', 'all')),
    17	  created_at timestamptz not null default now(),
    18	  updated_at timestamptz not null default now(),
    19	  -- Præcis én af area_id/page_id/tab_id skal være sat.
    20	  check (
    21	    (case when area_id is not null then 1 else 0 end) +
    22	    (case when page_id is not null then 1 else 0 end) +
    23	    (case when tab_id  is not null then 1 else 0 end) = 1
    24	  )
    25	);
    26	
    27	comment on table core_identity.role_permission_grants is
    28	  'T9 Step 7 V6 Beslutning 5: rettigheds-tildeling pr. (rolle × element). Præcis ét element-niveau (area/page/tab). visibility {self, subtree, all}.';

    31	create unique index role_permission_grants_unique

    49	-- ─── Helper: acl_subtree_org_nodes ──────────────────────────────────────
    50	-- Returnerer node_ids i caller's subtree (caller's placement-node + descendants via closure).
    51	create or replace function core_identity.acl_subtree_org_nodes(p_employee_id uuid)
    52	returns uuid[] language sql stable security invoker set search_path = '' as $$
    53	  select coalesce(array_agg(distinct c.descendant_id), '{}'::uuid[])
    54	  from core_identity.employee_node_placements p
    55	  join core_identity.org_node_closure c on c.ancestor_id = p.node_id
    56	  where p.employee_id = p_employee_id
    57	    and p.effective_from <= current_date
    58	    and (p.effective_to is null or p.effective_to > current_date);
    59	$$;
    60	comment on function core_identity.acl_subtree_org_nodes(uuid) is
    61	  'T9 Step 7: org_node-IDs i caller''s subtree. Plan V6 Valg 1+7. STABLE SECURITY INVOKER.';
    62	
    63	-- ─── Helper: acl_subtree_employees ──────────────────────────────────────
    64	create or replace function core_identity.acl_subtree_employees(p_employee_id uuid)
    65	returns uuid[] language sql stable security invoker set search_path = '' as $$
    66	  select coalesce(array_agg(distinct p.employee_id), '{}'::uuid[])
    67	  from core_identity.employee_node_placements p
    68	  where p.node_id = any(core_identity.acl_subtree_org_nodes(p_employee_id))
    69	    and p.effective_from <= current_date
    70	    and (p.effective_to is null or p.effective_to > current_date);
    71	$$;
    72	comment on function core_identity.acl_subtree_employees(uuid) is
    73	  'T9 Step 7: employee-IDs i caller''s subtree (placement på node i acl_subtree_org_nodes). Plan V6 Valg 1+7.';
    74	
    75	-- ─── Helper: permission_resolve ─────────────────────────────────────────
    76	-- Arve-aware lookup: tab → page → area → default-deny.
    77	create or replace function core_identity.permission_resolve(
    78	  p_role_id uuid,
    79	  p_element_type text,
    80	  p_element_id uuid
    81	) returns table (can_access boolean, can_write boolean, visibility text)
    82	language plpgsql stable security invoker set search_path = '' as $$
    83	declare
    84	  v_page_id uuid;
    85	  v_area_id uuid;
    86	  v_grant record;
    87	begin
    88	  -- Først: tab-niveau grant?
    89	  if p_element_type = 'tab' then
    90	    select * into v_grant from core_identity.role_permission_grants
    91	    where role_id = p_role_id and tab_id = p_element_id limit 1;
    92	    if found then
    93	      can_access := v_grant.can_access;
    94	      can_write := v_grant.can_write;
    95	      visibility := v_grant.visibility;
    96	      return next;
    97	      return;
    98	    end if;
    99	    -- Fald tilbage til page-niveau.
   100	    select page_id into v_page_id from core_identity.permission_tabs where id = p_element_id;
   101	  elsif p_element_type = 'page' then
   102	    v_page_id := p_element_id;
   103	  end if;
   104	
   105	  if v_page_id is not null then
   106	    select * into v_grant from core_identity.role_permission_grants
   107	    where role_id = p_role_id and page_id = v_page_id limit 1;
   108	    if found then
   109	      can_access := v_grant.can_access;
   110	      can_write := v_grant.can_write;
   111	      visibility := v_grant.visibility;
   112	      return next;
   113	      return;
   114	    end if;
   115	    -- Fald tilbage til area-niveau.
   116	    select area_id into v_area_id from core_identity.permission_pages where id = v_page_id;
   117	  end if;
   118	
   119	  if p_element_type = 'area' then
   120	    v_area_id := p_element_id;
   121	  end if;
   122	
   123	  if v_area_id is not null then
   124	    select * into v_grant from core_identity.role_permission_grants
   125	    where role_id = p_role_id and area_id = v_area_id limit 1;
   126	    if found then
   127	      can_access := v_grant.can_access;
   128	      can_write := v_grant.can_write;
   129	      visibility := v_grant.visibility;
   130	      return next;
   131	      return;
   132	    end if;
   133	  end if;
   134	
   135	  -- Default-deny.
   136	  can_access := false;
   137	  can_write := false;
   138	  visibility := 'self';
   139	  return next;
   140	end;
   141	$$;
   142	comment on function core_identity.permission_resolve(uuid, text, uuid) is
   143	  'T9 Step 7 Valg 6: arve-aware permission lookup (tab → page → area → default-deny). Plan V6.';
   144	
   145	-- ─── Helper: acl_visibility_check ───────────────────────────────────────
   146	-- V2 split (Codex V1 MELLEM): visibility-only; permission_resolve er separat.
   147	create or replace function core_identity.acl_visibility_check(
   148	  p_employee_id uuid,
   149	  p_target_id uuid,
   150	  p_target_kind text,
   151	  p_visibility text
   152	) returns boolean language sql stable security invoker set search_path = '' as $$
   153	  select case p_visibility
   154	    when 'all' then true
   155	    when 'self' then p_target_id = p_employee_id
   156	    when 'subtree' then
   157	      case p_target_kind
   158	        when 'employee' then p_target_id = any(core_identity.acl_subtree_employees(p_employee_id))
   159	        when 'org_node' then p_target_id = any(core_identity.acl_subtree_org_nodes(p_employee_id))
   160	        else false

 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	-- Trin 9 / §4 trin 9 Step 12: Seed Cph Sales + Ejere + Mathias/Kasper + superadmin-grants.
     2	--
     3	-- Plan V6 Valg 12 (V5-sweep): identity + version pair-pattern.
     4	-- mathias-afgoerelser pkt 1+18 + krav-dok 3.3.4: Mathias + Kasper på "Ejere"-afdeling.
     5	-- Eneste konkrete navne i krav-dokumentet (bootstrap, ikke fri valg).
     6	
     7	-- ─── FIX: has_permission record-syntaks-bug fra Step 11 (000009) ───────
     8	-- Step 11 deklarerede `v_grant record` og brugte `SELECT INTO v_grant.field`
     9	-- — Postgres tillader ikke INTO af individuelle record-felter før recorden
    10	-- som helhed er assigned. Manifesterede sig først ved DB-test af has_permission
    11	-- (record "v_grant" is not assigned yet, sqlstate 55000).
    12	--
    13	-- Step 11 er applied; immutability gælder. Fix via CREATE OR REPLACE her
    14	-- med individuelle bool-variabler i stedet for record.
    15	create or replace function core_identity.has_permission(
    16	  p_page_key text,
    17	  p_tab_key text default null,
    18	  p_can_edit boolean default false
    19	) returns boolean
    20	language plpgsql stable security invoker set search_path = ''
    21	as $hp$
    22	declare
    23	  v_employee_id uuid;
    24	  v_role_id uuid;
    25	  v_can_access boolean;
    26	  v_can_write boolean;
    27	begin
    28	  v_employee_id := core_identity.current_employee_id();
    29	  if v_employee_id is null then return false; end if;
    30	
    31	  select role_id into v_role_id from core_identity.employees where id = v_employee_id;
    32	  if v_role_id is null then return false; end if;
    33	
    34	  -- Ny model: resolve via grants (tab → page → area).
    35	  if p_tab_key is not null then
    36	    select g.can_access, g.can_write into v_can_access, v_can_write
    37	    from core_identity.role_permission_grants g
    38	    join core_identity.permission_tabs t on t.id = g.tab_id
    39	    join core_identity.permission_pages p on p.id = t.page_id
    40	    where g.role_id = v_role_id
    41	      and p.name = p_page_key
    42	      and t.name = p_tab_key
    43	    limit 1;
    44	    if found then
    45	      return v_can_access and (not p_can_edit or v_can_write);
    46	    end if;
    47	  end if;
    48	
    49	  -- Fald tilbage til page-niveau.
    50	  select g.can_access, g.can_write into v_can_access, v_can_write
    51	  from core_identity.role_permission_grants g
    52	  join core_identity.permission_pages p on p.id = g.page_id
    53	  where g.role_id = v_role_id and p.name = p_page_key
    54	  limit 1;
    55	  if found then
    56	    return v_can_access and (not p_can_edit or v_can_write);
    57	  end if;
    58	
    59	  -- Fald tilbage til area-niveau (via page-name → area).
    60	  select g.can_access, g.can_write into v_can_access, v_can_write
    61	  from core_identity.role_permission_grants g
    62	  join core_identity.permission_areas a on a.id = g.area_id
    63	  join core_identity.permission_pages p on p.area_id = a.id
    64	  where g.role_id = v_role_id and p.name = p_page_key
    65	  limit 1;
    66	  if found then
    67	    return v_can_access and (not p_can_edit or v_can_write);
    68	  end if;
    69	
    70	  -- Fallback til legacy role_page_permissions.
    71	  select can_view, can_edit into v_can_access, v_can_write
    72	  from core_identity.role_page_permissions
    73	  where role_id = v_role_id
    74	    and page_key = p_page_key
    75	    and (p_tab_key is null or tab_key = p_tab_key or tab_key is null)
    76	  order by case when tab_key = p_tab_key then 1 else 2 end
    77	  limit 1;
    78	
    79	  if found then
    80	    return v_can_access and (not p_can_edit or v_can_write);
    81	  end if;
    82	
    83	  return false;
    84	end;
    85	$hp$;
    86	
    87	-- ─── FIX: closure-rebuild CTE-bug fra Step 3 (000002) ──────────────────
    88	-- Step 3's rekursive CTE havde `join n.node_id = ac.descendant_id` (linje 71)
    89	-- i stedet for `ac.ancestor_id`. Det fik recursion til at gen-besøge samme
    90	-- (parent, child)-relation på alle depths 1..100 i stedet for at gå op til

    22	-- - KRITISK 4 Backdated effective_from guards på 5 apply-handlers

    25	
    26	-- ─── DEL 0: GRANT INSERT/UPDATE/DELETE på 6 write-tabeller ────────────────
    27	--
    28	-- Codex runde 3 fund 1: RLS policy er ortogonal til SQL-privileges. T9
    29	-- migrations gjorde `revoke all` + `grant select to authenticated`. Uden
    30	-- explicit INSERT/UPDATE/DELETE-grant vil RPC-write fejle MED "permission
    31	-- denied for table" FØR session-var-policy kan evaluere. Pre-T9 (R1B, P1a)
    32	-- fulgte begge mønstre konsekvent.
    33	
    34	grant insert, update on table core_identity.pending_changes to authenticated;
    35	grant insert, update on table core_identity.undo_settings to authenticated;
    36	grant insert, update on table core_identity.permission_areas to authenticated;
    37	grant insert, update on table core_identity.permission_pages to authenticated;
    38	grant insert, update on table core_identity.permission_tabs to authenticated;
    39	grant insert, update, delete on table core_identity.role_permission_grants to authenticated;
    40	
    41	-- ─── DEL 1: Policies på 6 write-tabeller ──────────────────────────────────
    42	--
    43	-- Pattern: INSERT-policy med WITH CHECK + UPDATE-policy med USING.
    44	-- Begge kræver current_setting('stork.t9_write_authorized', true) = 'true'.
    45	-- Tredje arg til current_setting('...', true) returnerer NULL hvis var ikke
    46	-- er sat — koalescerer til false i bool-sammenligning.
    47	
    48	-- 1.1 pending_changes
    49	create policy pending_changes_insert on core_identity.pending_changes
    50	  for insert to authenticated
    51	  with check (current_setting('stork.t9_write_authorized', true) = 'true');
    52	
    53	create policy pending_changes_update on core_identity.pending_changes
    54	  for update to authenticated
    55	  using (current_setting('stork.t9_write_authorized', true) = 'true');
    56	
    57	-- Codex runde 3 fund 2: SELECT-policy fra Step 1 (Step 1's body linje 87-93)
    58	-- tillod kun requester + is_admin() at se pending rows. Det blokerer
    59	-- pending_change_approve/undo's dispatcher (select * ... for update køres
    60	-- FØR dispatcher kan evaluere has_permission). Erstat med policy der også
    61	-- tillader potentielle approvere/undoere baseret på samme change_type →
    62	-- page_key-mapping som dispatcheren bruger. Holder §1.1: policy er
    63	-- write-uafhængig; dispatcher gates'er write som sandhed.
    64	drop policy if exists pending_changes_select on core_identity.pending_changes;
    65	
    66	create policy pending_changes_select on core_identity.pending_changes
    67	  for select to authenticated
    68	  using (
    69	    requested_by = core_identity.current_employee_id()
    70	    or core_identity.is_admin()
    71	    or (
    72	      change_type in ('org_node_upsert', 'org_node_deactivate', 'team_close')
    73	        and core_identity.has_permission('org_nodes', null, true)
    74	    )
    75	    or (
    76	      change_type in ('employee_place', 'employee_remove')
    77	        and core_identity.has_permission('employee_placements', null, true)
    78	    )
    79	    or (
    80	      change_type in ('client_place', 'client_close')
    81	        and core_identity.has_permission('client_placements', null, true)
    82	    )
    83	  );
    84	
    85	-- 1.2 undo_settings
    86	create policy undo_settings_insert on core_identity.undo_settings
    87	  for insert to authenticated
    88	  with check (current_setting('stork.t9_write_authorized', true) = 'true');
    89	
    90	create policy undo_settings_update on core_identity.undo_settings
    91	  for update to authenticated
    92	  using (current_setting('stork.t9_write_authorized', true) = 'true');
    93

    96	  for insert to authenticated

   100	  for update to authenticated
   101	  using (current_setting('stork.t9_write_authorized', true) = 'true');
   102	
   103	-- 1.4 permission_pages

   107

   125	-- role_permission_grant_remove udfører faktisk DELETE under FORCE RLS fra

   139	-- ─── DEL 2: 11 write-RPCs får session-var pattern ─────────────────────────
   140	--
   141	-- Pattern per RPC:
   142	--   1. has_permission-check (defense-in-depth, FØR autorisation)
   143	--   2. perform set_config('stork.t9_write_authorized', 'true', true)
   144	--      (true = local til transaktion; var lækker ikke)
   145	--   3. Eksisterende set_config'er for audit (stork.source_type, stork.change_reason)
   146	--   4. Selve INSERT/UPDATE
   147	
   148	-- 2.1 pending_change_approve (Step 1, UPDATE pending_changes)
   149	--
   150	-- Mathias 2026-05-19 (T9-omstart-rammen punkt 12): Approve er ikke ny adgang.
   151	-- Den er can_edit på den ressource som pending change rammer. Hvis bruger har
   152	-- can_edit=true på org_træ-area, må vedkommende også approve en pending change
   153	-- der ændrer org_træ.
   154	--
   155	-- Dispatcher-mapping change_type → has_permission(page_key, can_edit=true):
   156	--   org_node_upsert     → 'org_nodes'           (struktur-ændring af knude)
   157	--   org_node_deactivate → 'org_nodes'           (struktur-ændring af knude)
   158	--   team_close          → 'org_nodes'           (lukker team-knude — struktur)
   159	--   employee_place      → 'employee_placements' (medarbejder-placering)
   160	--   employee_remove     → 'employee_placements' (medarbejder-placering)
