   118	-- ─── RPC: pending_change_request (INTERN; kaldes kun af public wrappers) ──
   119	-- V3 Beslutning 12: pending_change_request er INTERN. Public wrappers (Step 8)
   120	-- er SECURITY DEFINER og er ENESTE indgang. Direct authenticated-kald afvises.
   121	create or replace function core_identity.pending_change_request(
   122	  p_change_type text,
   123	  p_target_id uuid,
   124	  p_payload jsonb,
   125	  p_effective_from date
   126	) returns uuid
   127	language plpgsql
   128	security invoker
   129	set search_path = ''
   130	as $$
   131	declare
   132	  v_request_id uuid;
   133	  v_requested_by uuid;
   134	begin
   135	  v_requested_by := core_identity.current_employee_id();
   136	  if v_requested_by is null then
   137	    raise exception 'no_authenticated_employee'
   138	      using errcode = '42501', hint = 'pending_change_request kræver authenticated employee';
   139	  end if;
   140	
   141	  -- INSERT med eksplicit session-vars (audit-trigger fanger).
   142	  perform set_config('stork.source_type', 'manual', true);
   143	  perform set_config('stork.change_reason', 'pending_change_request', true);
   144	
   145	  insert into core_identity.pending_changes
   146	    (change_type, target_id, payload, effective_from, requested_by, status)
   147	  values
   148	    (p_change_type, p_target_id, p_payload, p_effective_from, v_requested_by, 'pending')
   149	  returning id into v_request_id;
   150	
   151	  return v_request_id;
   152	end;
   153	$$;
   154

   161	-- ─── RPC: pending_change_approve ─────────────────────────────────────────
   162	create or replace function core_identity.pending_change_approve(
   163	  p_change_id uuid
   164	) returns void
   165	language plpgsql
   166	security invoker
   167	set search_path = ''
   168	as $$
   169	declare
   170	  v_change record;
   171	  v_approver uuid;
   172	  v_undo_period integer;
   173	begin
   174	  v_approver := core_identity.current_employee_id();
   175	  if v_approver is null then
   176	    raise exception 'no_authenticated_employee'
   177	      using errcode = '42501';
   178	  end if;
   179	
   180	  select * into v_change
   181	  from core_identity.pending_changes
   182	  where id = p_change_id
   183	  for update;
   184	
   185	  if not found then
   186	    raise exception 'pending_change_not_found %', p_change_id
   187	      using errcode = 'P0002';
   188	  end if;
   189	
   190	  if v_change.status <> 'pending' then
   191	    raise exception 'pending_change_wrong_status: % (expected pending)', v_change.status
   192	      using errcode = '22023';
   193	  end if;
   194	
   195	  if v_change.requested_by = v_approver and not core_identity.is_admin() then
   196	    raise exception 'pending_change_self_approve_forbidden'
   197	      using errcode = '42501', hint = 'requester må ikke selv approve (medmindre admin)';
   198	  end if;
   199	
   200	  -- Hent undo-periode fra konfig.
   201	  select undo_period_seconds into v_undo_period
   202	  from core_identity.undo_settings
   203	  where change_type = v_change.change_type;
   204	
   205	  if v_undo_period is null then
   206	    -- Default 24t hvis ingen konfig (defensiv).
   207	    v_undo_period := 24 * 3600;
   208	  end if;
   209	
   210	  perform set_config('stork.source_type', 'manual', true);
   211	  perform set_config('stork.change_reason', 'pending_change_approve', true);
   212	
   213	  update core_identity.pending_changes
   214	  set status = 'approved',
   215	      approved_by = v_approver,
   216	      approved_at = now(),
   217	      undo_deadline = now() + (v_undo_period || ' seconds')::interval,
   218	      updated_at = now()
   219	  where id = p_change_id;
   220	end;
   221	$$;
   222	
   223	comment on function core_identity.pending_change_approve(uuid) is
   224	  'T9 Step 1: godkender pending; sætter undo_deadline = now() + undo_settings.undo_period_seconds.';
   225	
   226	revoke execute on function core_identity.pending_change_approve(uuid) from public, anon;
   227	
   228	-- ─── RPC: pending_change_undo ────────────────────────────────────────────
   229	create or replace function core_identity.pending_change_undo(
   230	  p_change_id uuid
   231	) returns void
   232	language plpgsql
   233	security invoker
   234	set search_path = ''
   235	as $$
   236	declare
   237	  v_change record;
   238	begin
   239	  select * into v_change
   240	  from core_identity.pending_changes
   241	  where id = p_change_id
   242	  for update;
   243	
   244	  if not found then
   245	    raise exception 'pending_change_not_found %', p_change_id
   246	      using errcode = 'P0002';
   247	  end if;
   248	
   249	  if v_change.status <> 'approved' then
   250	    raise exception 'pending_change_wrong_status: % (expected approved)', v_change.status
   251	      using errcode = '22023';
   252	  end if;
   253	
   254	  if v_change.undo_deadline <= now() then
   255	    raise exception 'undo_deadline_expired'
   256	      using errcode = '22023',
   257	            hint = format('deadline var %s', v_change.undo_deadline);
   258	  end if;
   259	
   260	  perform set_config('stork.source_type', 'manual', true);
   261	  perform set_config('stork.change_reason', 'pending_change_undo', true);
   262	
   263	  update core_identity.pending_changes
   264	  set status = 'undone',
   265	      undone_at = now(),
   266	      updated_at = now()
   267	  where id = p_change_id;
   268	end;
   269	$$;
   270

   272	  'T9 Step 1: ruller approved-row tilbage før undo_deadline. Efter deadline: exception.';

   276	-- ─── RPC: pending_change_apply (CENTRAL APPLY-GATE — V6 Beslutning 15) ────
   277	-- V6 Codex KRITISK-fix: sikkerheds-grænsen for "ikke materialiser future-dated"
   278	-- sidder HER, ikke kun i cron-filter. ALLE apply-paths (cron, manuel admin, test)
   279	-- går gennem samme gate.
   280	create or replace function core_identity.pending_change_apply(
   281	  p_change_id uuid
   282	) returns void
   283	language plpgsql
   284	security definer
   285	set search_path = ''
   286	as $$
   287	declare
   288	  v_change record;
   289	begin
   290	  select * into v_change
   291	  from core_identity.pending_changes
   292	  where id = p_change_id
   293	  for update;
   294	
   295	  if not found then
   296	    raise exception 'pending_change_not_found %', p_change_id
   297	      using errcode = 'P0002';
   298	  end if;
   299	
   300	  -- V6 central apply-gate: due-check.
   301	  if v_change.status <> 'approved' then
   302	    raise exception 'pending_change_not_approved: status=%', v_change.status
   303	      using errcode = '22023';
   304	  end if;
   305	
   306	  if v_change.undo_deadline > now() then
   307	    raise exception 'not_yet_due'
   308	      using errcode = '22023',
   309	            hint = format('undo_deadline=%s, now=%s', v_change.undo_deadline, now());
   310	  end if;
   311	
   312	  if v_change.effective_from > current_date then
   313	    raise exception 'not_yet_due'
   314	      using errcode = '22023',
   315	            hint = format('effective_from=%s, current_date=%s', v_change.effective_from, current_date);
   316	  end if;
   317	
   318	  perform set_config('stork.source_type', 'manual', true);
   319	  perform set_config('stork.change_reason', 'pending_change_apply', true);
   320	
   321	  -- Dispatcher: switch på change_type til intern handler.
   322	  -- Steps 2+4+5 udvider via CREATE OR REPLACE af denne funktion med rigtige
   323	  -- CASE WHEN-handlers. I Step 1 er der ingen handlers, så vi raiser direkte.
   324	  raise exception 'unknown_change_type: %', v_change.change_type
   325	    using errcode = '42883',
   326	          hint = 'Step 1 dispatcher har ingen handlers; Steps 2+4+5 udvider via CREATE OR REPLACE';
   327	
   328	  -- Når Steps 2+4+5 udvider CASE: mark applied her efter handler returnerer.
   329	  update core_identity.pending_changes
   330	  set status = 'applied',
   331	      applied_at = now(),
   332	      updated_at = now()
   333	  where id = p_change_id;
   334	end;
   335	$$;
   336	
   337	comment on function core_identity.pending_change_apply(uuid) is
   338	  'T9 Step 1: CENTRAL APPLY-GATE. V6 Beslutning 15. Verificerer due-check (status=approved AND undo_deadline <= now() AND effective_from <= current_date). Hvis ikke: RAISE not_yet_due. Dispatcher til intern handler. Eksekveres af cron eller manuelt af admin; ALLE paths gennem samme gate.';
   339	
   340	revoke execute on function core_identity.pending_change_apply(uuid) from public, anon;

    57	-- ─── Team-only validering ────────────────────────────────────────────────
    58	create or replace function core_identity._client_placement_team_check()
    59	returns trigger
    60	language plpgsql
    61	security invoker
    62	set search_path = ''
    63	as $$
    64	begin
    65	  -- Verificér at node_id refererer til team-knude (current version).
    66	  if not exists (
    67	    select 1 from core_identity.org_node_versions
    68	    where node_id = new.node_id
    69	      and node_type = 'team'
    70	      and effective_from <= new.effective_from
    71	      and (effective_to is null or effective_to > new.effective_from)
    72	  ) then
    73	    raise exception 'client_placement_node_not_team: % er ikke team-knude på effective_from %', new.node_id, new.effective_from
    74	      using errcode = 'P0001';
    75	  end if;
    76	
    77	  return new;
    78	end;
    79	$$;

    82	  before insert or update on core_identity.client_node_placements

    86	create or replace function core_identity._apply_client_place(
    87	  p_payload jsonb,
    88	  p_pending_change_id uuid
    89	) returns void
    90	language plpgsql
    91	security definer
    92	set search_path = ''
    93	as $$
    94	declare
    95	  v_client_id uuid;
    96	  v_node_id uuid;
    97	  v_effective_from date;
    98	begin
    99	  v_client_id := (p_payload->>'client_id')::uuid;
   100	  v_node_id := (p_payload->>'node_id')::uuid;
   101	  v_effective_from := (p_payload->>'effective_from')::date;
   102	
   103	  if v_client_id is null or v_node_id is null or v_effective_from is null then
   104	    raise exception 'invalid_payload: client_id + node_id + effective_from required'
   105	      using errcode = '22023';
   106	  end if;
   107	
   108	  -- Luk eventuel åben placement (flyt).
   109	  update core_identity.client_node_placements
   110	  set effective_to = v_effective_from, updated_at = now()
   111	  where client_id = v_client_id and effective_to is null;
   112	
   113	  -- Åbn ny placement (trigger validerer team-only).
   114	  insert into core_identity.client_node_placements
   115	    (client_id, node_id, effective_from, effective_to, created_by_pending_change_id)
   116	  values
   117	    (v_client_id, v_node_id, v_effective_from, null, p_pending_change_id);
   118	end;
   119	$$;

   127	language plpgsql

   131	declare
   132	  v_client_id uuid;

   134	begin
   135	  v_client_id := (p_payload->>'client_id')::uuid;
   136	  v_effective_from := (p_payload->>'effective_from')::date;
   137	
   138	  if v_client_id is null or v_effective_from is null then
   139	    raise exception 'invalid_payload: client_id + effective_from required'
   140	      using errcode = '22023';
   141	  end if;
   142	
   143	  update core_identity.client_node_placements
   144	  set effective_to = v_effective_from, updated_at = now()
   145	  where client_id = v_client_id and effective_to is null;
   146	end;
   147	$$;
   148	
   149	revoke execute on function core_identity._apply_client_close(jsonb, uuid) from public, anon, authenticated;
   150	
   151	-- ─── CREATE OR REPLACE pending_change_apply: tilføj 2 cases ─────────────
   152	create or replace function core_identity.pending_change_apply(
   153	  p_change_id uuid
   154	) returns void
   155	language plpgsql
   156	security definer
   157	set search_path = ''
   158	as $$
   159	declare
   160	  v_change record;
   161	begin
   162	  select * into v_change
   163	  from core_identity.pending_changes
   164	  where id = p_change_id
   165	  for update;
   166	
   167	  if not found then
   168	    raise exception 'pending_change_not_found %', p_change_id
   169	      using errcode = 'P0002';
   170	  end if;
   171	
   172	  if v_change.status <> 'approved' then
   173	    raise exception 'pending_change_not_approved: status=%', v_change.status
   174	      using errcode = '22023';
   175	  end if;
   176	
   177	  if v_change.undo_deadline > now() then
   178	    raise exception 'not_yet_due'
   179	      using errcode = '22023',
   180	            hint = format('undo_deadline=%s, now=%s', v_change.undo_deadline, now());
   181	  end if;
   182	
   183	  if v_change.effective_from > current_date then
   184	    raise exception 'not_yet_due'
   185	      using errcode = '22023',
   186	            hint = format('effective_from=%s, current_date=%s', v_change.effective_from, current_date);
   187	  end if;
   188	
   189	  perform set_config('stork.source_type', 'manual', true);
   190	  perform set_config('stork.change_reason', 'pending_change_apply', true);
   191	
   192	  case v_change.change_type
   193	    when 'org_node_upsert' then
   194	      perform core_identity._apply_org_node_upsert(v_change.payload, p_change_id);
   195	    when 'org_node_deactivate' then
   196	      perform core_identity._apply_org_node_deactivate(v_change.payload, p_change_id);
   197	    when 'employee_place' then
   198	      perform core_identity._apply_employee_place(v_change.payload, p_change_id);
   199	    when 'employee_remove' then
   200	      perform core_identity._apply_employee_remove(v_change.payload, p_change_id);
   201	    when 'team_close' then
   202	      perform core_identity._apply_team_close(v_change.payload, p_change_id);
   203	    when 'client_place' then
   204	      perform core_identity._apply_client_place(v_change.payload, p_change_id);
   205	    when 'client_close' then
   206	      perform core_identity._apply_client_close(v_change.payload, p_change_id);
   207	    else
   208	      raise exception 'unknown_change_type: %', v_change.change_type
   209	        using errcode = '42883';
   210	  end case;
   211	
   212	  update core_identity.pending_changes
   213	  set status = 'applied',
   214	      applied_at = now(),
   215	      updated_at = now()
   216	  where id = p_change_id;
   217	end;
   218	$$;
   219	
   220	revoke execute on function core_identity.pending_change_apply(uuid) from public, anon;
   221	
   222	-- ─── Seed undo_settings ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
   223	select set_config('stork.source_type', 'migration', false);
   224	select set_config('stork.change_reason', 'T9 Step 5: seed undo_settings for client_place/close', false);
   225	
   226	insert into core_identity.undo_settings (change_type, undo_period_seconds)
   227	values
   228	  ('client_place', 24 * 3600),
   229	  ('client_close', 24 * 3600)
   230	on conflict (change_type) do nothing;

   272	    return;

   277	    where id = v_active.id;

   284	-- ─── _apply_client_place (place-handler) ──────────────────────────────────
   285	create or replace function core_identity._apply_client_place(
   286	  p_payload jsonb,
   287	  p_pending_change_id uuid
   288	) returns void
   289	language plpgsql
   290	security definer
   291	set search_path = ''
   292	as $$
   293	declare
   294	  v_client_id uuid;
   295	  v_node_id uuid;
   296	  v_effective_from date;
   297	  v_active record;
   298	begin
   299	  v_client_id := (p_payload->>'client_id')::uuid;
   300	  v_node_id := (p_payload->>'node_id')::uuid;
   301	  v_effective_from := (p_payload->>'effective_from')::date;
   302	
   303	  if v_client_id is null or v_node_id is null or v_effective_from is null then
   304	    raise exception 'invalid_payload: client_id + node_id + effective_from required'
   305	      using errcode = '22023';
   306	  end if;
   307	
   308	  -- Verificér node er team + aktiv på v_effective_from.
   309	  if not exists (
   310	    select 1 from core_identity.org_node_versions
   311	    where node_id = v_node_id
   312	      and node_type = 'team'
   313	      and is_active = true
   314	      and effective_from <= v_effective_from
   315	      and (effective_to is null or effective_to > v_effective_from)
   316	  ) then
   317	    raise exception 'client_placement_requires_active_team: %', v_node_id
   318	      using errcode = 'P0001';
   319	  end if;
   320	
   321	  select * into v_active
   322	  from core_identity.client_node_placements
   323	  where client_id = v_client_id
   324	    and effective_from <= v_effective_from
   325	    and (effective_to is null or effective_to > v_effective_from)
   326	  limit 1;
   327	
   328	  if not found then
   329	    insert into core_identity.client_node_placements
   330	      (client_id, node_id, effective_from, effective_to, created_by_pending_change_id)
   331	    select v_client_id, v_node_id, v_effective_from,
   332	      (select min(effective_from) from core_identity.client_node_placements
   333	       where client_id = v_client_id and effective_from > v_effective_from),
   334	      p_pending_change_id;
   335	  elsif v_active.effective_from = v_effective_from then
   336	    update core_identity.client_node_placements
   337	    set node_id = v_node_id,
   338	        created_by_pending_change_id = coalesce(p_pending_change_id, created_by_pending_change_id),
   339	        updated_at = now()
   340	    where id = v_active.id;
   341	  else
   342	    update core_identity.client_node_placements
   343	    set effective_to = v_effective_from, updated_at = now()
   344	    where id = v_active.id;
   345	
   346	    insert into core_identity.client_node_placements
   347	      (client_id, node_id, effective_from, effective_to, created_by_pending_change_id)
   348	    values
   349	      (v_client_id, v_node_id, v_effective_from, v_active.effective_to, p_pending_change_id);
   350	  end if;
   351	end;
   352	$$;
   353	
   354	revoke execute on function core_identity._apply_client_place(jsonb, uuid) from public, anon, authenticated;
   355

   357	create or replace function core_identity._apply_client_close(
   358	  p_payload jsonb,
   359	  p_pending_change_id uuid
   360	) returns void

   403	  p_payload jsonb,
   404	  p_pending_change_id uuid
   405	) returns void
   406	language plpgsql
   407	security definer

   410	declare

   414	  v_node_type text;

   418	  v_active record;
   419	begin
   420	  v_node_id := nullif(p_payload->>'id', '')::uuid;
   421	  v_name := p_payload->>'name';
   422	  v_parent_id := nullif(p_payload->>'parent_id', '')::uuid;
   423	  v_node_type := p_payload->>'node_type';
   424	  v_is_active := coalesce((p_payload->>'is_active')::boolean, true);
   425	  v_effective_from := (p_payload->>'effective_from')::date;
   426	
   427	  if v_name is null or v_node_type is null or v_effective_from is null then
   428	    raise exception 'invalid_payload: name + node_type + effective_from required'
   429	      using errcode = '22023';
   430	  end if;

   658	-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   659	-- SECTION C2 — Udvidet SELECT-policy på client_node_placements (Step 3b)
   660	-- ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   661	-- Codex V2 KRITISK 2 fix. Nuværende policy `using (is_admin())` blokerer
   662	-- non-admin reads før RPC kan filtrere. V4-fix: bruger session-var
   663	-- stork.t9_read_at_date (default current_date) som date-parameter til ACL.
   664	
   665	drop policy if exists client_node_placements_select on core_identity.client_node_placements;
   666	
   667	create policy client_node_placements_select on core_identity.client_node_placements
   668	  for select to authenticated
   669	  using (
   670	    core_identity.is_admin()
   671	    or node_id = ANY(
   672	      core_identity.acl_subtree_org_nodes_at(
   673	        core_identity.current_employee_id(),
   674	        coalesce(
   675	          nullif(current_setting('stork.t9_read_at_date', true), '')::date,
   676	          current_date
   677	        )
   678	      )
   679	    )
   680	  );
   681

   683	  'T9-supplement Step 3b: superadmin ser alt; ellers scoped via acl_subtree_org_nodes_at med session-var stork.t9_read_at_date (default current_date).';

   748	-- Bevarer Step 9's signatur; tilføjer kun _require_read_permission-gate.
   749	create or replace function core_identity.role_permissions_read(p_role_id uuid)
   750	returns table (
   751	  grant_id uuid,
   752	  element_type text,
   753	  element_id uuid,
   754	  element_name text,
   755	  can_access boolean,
   756	  can_write boolean,
   757	  visibility text
   758	)
   759	language plpgsql
   760	stable
   761	security invoker
   762	set search_path = ''
   763	as $$
   764	begin
   765	  perform core_identity._require_read_permission('permissions', 'manage');
   766	
   767	  return query
   768	  select g.id, 'area'::text, g.area_id, a.name, g.can_access, g.can_write, g.visibility
   769	  from core_identity.role_permission_grants g
   770	  join core_identity.permission_areas a on a.id = g.area_id
   771	  where g.role_id = p_role_id and g.area_id is not null
   772	  union all
   773	  select g.id, 'page'::text, g.page_id, p.name, g.can_access, g.can_write, g.visibility
   774	  from core_identity.role_permission_grants g
   775	  join core_identity.permission_pages p on p.id = g.page_id
   776	  where g.role_id = p_role_id and g.page_id is not null
   777	  union all
   778	  select g.id, 'tab'::text, g.tab_id, t.name, g.can_access, g.can_write, g.visibility
   779	  from core_identity.role_permission_grants g
   780	  join core_identity.permission_tabs t on t.id = g.tab_id
   781	  where g.role_id = p_role_id and g.tab_id is not null;
   782	end;
   783	$$;
   784	
   785	revoke execute on function core_identity.role_permissions_read(uuid) from public, anon;
   786	grant execute on function core_identity.role_permissions_read(uuid) to authenticated;

    13	-- ændringer i has_permission-logik, andre roller, eller Q-SEED.

    15	-- MAPPING change_type → (page, tab) matcher
    16	-- T9-fundament-supplement (PR #39) pending_change_approve/undo
    17	-- dispatcher-mappingen:
    18	--   page=org_nodes           — org_node_upsert/deactivate, team_close

    20	--   page=client_placements   — client_node_place, client_node_close

    31	  'M1-fix: seed superadmin permission-rows for T9 write-RPCs', false);

    34	  (role_id, page_key, tab_key, can_view, can_edit, scope)

    36	       page_key, tab_key, can_view, can_edit, 'all'
    37	from (values

    39	  ('org_nodes',           'manage',   true, true),

    42	  -- T9 client-placement-RPCs (client_node_place, client_node_close)

    44	  -- T9 permission-element-CRUDs + grant-RPCs

    46	  -- T9 undo-settings-konfig (undo_setting_update)
    47	  ('pending_changes',     'settings', true, true)

 succeeded in 0ms:
    94	-- ─── Migrér eksisterende role_page_permissions til role_permission_grants ─
    95	do $seed$
    96	declare
    97	  v_row record;
    98	  v_area_id uuid;
    99	  v_page_id uuid;
   100	  v_tab_id uuid;
   101	  v_visibility text;
   102	begin
   103	  for v_row in select * from core_identity.role_page_permissions
   104	  loop
   105	    -- Map scope → visibility (team → subtree).
   106	    v_visibility := case v_row.scope
   107	      when 'all' then 'all'
   108	      when 'self' then 'self'
   109	      when 'subtree' then 'subtree'
   110	      when 'team' then 'subtree'  -- V5 mathias-afgoerelser pkt 14: team udgår
   111	      else 'self'
   112	    end;
   113	
   114	    -- Find element-niveau (tab hvis ikke-NULL, ellers page).
   115	    if v_row.tab_key is not null then
   116	      select t.id into v_tab_id
   117	      from core_identity.permission_tabs t
   118	      join core_identity.permission_pages p on p.id = t.page_id
   119	      where p.name = v_row.page_key and t.name = v_row.tab_key;
   120	
   121	      insert into core_identity.role_permission_grants
   122	        (role_id, area_id, page_id, tab_id, can_access, can_write, visibility)
   123	      values
   124	        (v_row.role_id, null, null, v_tab_id, v_row.can_view, v_row.can_edit, v_visibility)
   125	      on conflict (role_id, coalesce(area_id::text, ''), coalesce(page_id::text, ''), coalesce(tab_id::text, ''))
   126	      do nothing;
   127	    else
   128	      select id into v_page_id from core_identity.permission_pages
   129	      where name = v_row.page_key;
   130	
   131	      insert into core_identity.role_permission_grants
   132	        (role_id, area_id, page_id, tab_id, can_access, can_write, visibility)
   133	      values
   134	        (v_row.role_id, null, v_page_id, null, v_row.can_view, v_row.can_edit, v_visibility)
   135	      on conflict (role_id, coalesce(area_id::text, ''), coalesce(page_id::text, ''), coalesce(tab_id::text, ''))
   136	      do nothing;
   137	    end if;
   138	  end loop;
   139	end;
   140	$seed$;
   141	
   142	-- ─── has_permission() opdateres med ny model + fallback ─────────────────
   143	-- Plan V6 Valg 11: helpers læser fra role_permission_grants med fallback til
   144	-- role_page_permissions (legacy read-only). Fallback fjernes når sidste
   145	-- konsument er migreret (G-nummer i Step 13).
   146	
   147	create or replace function core_identity.has_permission(
   148	  p_page_key text,
   149	  p_tab_key text default null,
   150	  p_can_edit boolean default false
   151	) returns boolean
   152	language plpgsql stable security invoker set search_path = ''
   153	as $$
   154	declare
   155	  v_employee_id uuid;
   156	  v_role_id uuid;
   157	  v_grant record;
   158	begin
   159	  v_employee_id := core_identity.current_employee_id();
   160	  if v_employee_id is null then return false; end if;
   161	
   162	  select role_id into v_role_id from core_identity.employees where id = v_employee_id;
   163	  if v_role_id is null then return false; end if;
   164	
   165	  -- Ny model: resolve via grants (tab → page → area).
   166	  if p_tab_key is not null then
   167	    select g.can_access, g.can_write into v_grant.can_access, v_grant.can_write
   168	    from core_identity.role_permission_grants g
   169	    join core_identity.permission_tabs t on t.id = g.tab_id
   170	    join core_identity.permission_pages p on p.id = t.page_id
   171	    where g.role_id = v_role_id
   172	      and p.name = p_page_key
   173	      and t.name = p_tab_key
   174	    limit 1;
   175	    if found then
   176	      return v_grant.can_access and (not p_can_edit or v_grant.can_write);
   177	    end if;
   178	  end if;
   179	
   180	  -- Fald tilbage til page-niveau.
   181	  select g.can_access, g.can_write into v_grant.can_access, v_grant.can_write
   182	  from core_identity.role_permission_grants g
   183	  join core_identity.permission_pages p on p.id = g.page_id
   184	  where g.role_id = v_role_id and p.name = p_page_key
   185	  limit 1;
   186	  if found then
   187	    return v_grant.can_access and (not p_can_edit or v_grant.can_write);
   188	  end if;
   189	
   190	  -- Fald tilbage til area-niveau (via page-name → area).
   191	  select g.can_access, g.can_write into v_grant.can_access, v_grant.can_write
   192	  from core_identity.role_permission_grants g
   193	  join core_identity.permission_areas a on a.id = g.area_id
   194	  join core_identity.permission_pages p on p.area_id = a.id
   195	  where g.role_id = v_role_id and p.name = p_page_key
   196	  limit 1;
   197	  if found then
   198	    return v_grant.can_access and (not p_can_edit or v_grant.can_write);
   199	  end if;
   200	
   201	  -- Fallback til legacy role_page_permissions (G-nummer for senere pakke-drop).
   202	  select can_view, can_edit into v_grant.can_access, v_grant.can_write
   203	  from core_identity.role_page_permissions
   204	  where role_id = v_role_id
   205	    and page_key = p_page_key
   206	    and (p_tab_key is null or tab_key = p_tab_key or tab_key is null)
   207	  order by case when tab_key = p_tab_key then 1 else 2 end
   208	  limit 1;
   209	
   210	  if found then
   211	    return v_grant.can_access and (not p_can_edit or v_grant.can_write);
   212	  end if;
   213	
   214	  return false;
   215	end;
   216	$$;
   217	
   218	comment on function core_identity.has_permission(text, text, boolean) is
   219	  'T9 Step 11 V6 Valg 11: opdateret med role_permission_grants som primær + fallback til legacy role_page_permissions. Fallback fjernes når alle konsumenter er migreret (G-nummer for senere pakke).';
   220

 succeeded in 0ms:
    56	create or replace function core_identity.enforce_admin_floor()
    57	returns trigger
    58	language plpgsql
    59	security definer
    60	set search_path = ''
    61	as $$
    62	declare
    63	  v_active_admins integer;
    64	  v_min_admins integer;
    65	begin
    66	  select min_admin_count into v_min_admins
    67	    from core_compliance.superadmin_settings where id = 1;
    68	
    69	  select count(*) into v_active_admins
    70	    from core_identity.employees e
    71	    join core_identity.role_page_permissions p on p.role_id = e.role_id
    72	   where e.anonymized_at is null
    73	     and p.page_key = 'system'
    74	     and p.tab_key = 'manage'
    75	     and p.scope = 'all'
    76	     and p.can_edit = true;
    77	
    78	  if v_active_admins < v_min_admins then
    79	    raise exception 'superadmin-floor overtrådt: % aktive admins er under minimum %', v_active_admins, v_min_admins
    80	      using errcode = 'P0001',
    81	            hint = 'Mindst ' || v_min_admins || ' admin-medarbejdere skal bevares. Tilføj ny admin før denne ændring.';
    82	  end if;
    83	
    84	  return null;  -- AFTER-trigger
    85	end;
    86	$$;

/bin/bash -lc "nl -ba supabase/migrations/20260514180300_q1_employee_active_config.sql | sed -n '128,162p'" in /home/mathias/stork-2.0
 succeeded in 0ms:
   128	$$;
   129	
   130	-- ─── Refactor is_admin() ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
   131	create or replace function core_identity.is_admin()
   132	returns boolean
   133	language sql stable security invoker set search_path = ''
   134	as $$
   135	  select exists (
   136	    select 1
   137	    from core_identity.employees e
   138	    join core_identity.role_page_permissions p on p.role_id = e.role_id
   139	    where e.auth_user_id = auth.uid()
   140	      and core_identity.is_active_employee_state(e.anonymized_at, e.termination_date)
   141	      and p.page_key = 'system'
   142	      and p.tab_key = 'manage'
   143	      and p.scope = 'all'
   144	      and p.can_edit = true
   145	  );
   146	$$;
   147	
   148	-- ─── Refactor enforce_admin_floor() ────────────────────────────────────────
   149	create or replace function core_identity.enforce_admin_floor()
   150	returns trigger
   151	language plpgsql security definer set search_path = ''
   152	as $func$
   153	declare
   154	  v_active_admins integer;
   155	  v_min_admins integer;
   156	begin
   157	  select min_admin_count into v_min_admins
   158	    from core_compliance.superadmin_settings where id = 1;
   159	
   160	  select count(*) into v_active_admins
   161	    from core_identity.employees e
   162	    join core_identity.role_page_permissions p on p.role_id = e.role_id

    81	  end if;

    83	  -- ─── T2: _apply_employee_place på allerede placeret (flyt) ────────────
    84	  perform core_identity._apply_employee_place(
    85	    jsonb_build_object('employee_id', v_emp_a_id::text, 'node_id', v_team_b_id::text, 'effective_from', current_date::text),
    86	    null
    87	  );
    88	
    89	  -- Count filter på fixture-employee (ikke global state).
    90	  select count(*) into v_count
    91	  from core_identity.employee_node_placements
    92	  where employee_id = v_emp_a_id;
    93	  if v_count <> 2 then
    94	    raise exception 'T2 FAIL: flyt skal give 2 rows for fixture-employee (lukket+åben), got %', v_count;
    95	  end if;
    96	
    97	  if not exists (
    98	    select 1 from core_identity.employee_node_placements
    99	    where employee_id = v_emp_a_id and node_id = v_team_b_id and effective_to is null
   100	  ) then
   101	    raise exception 'T2 FAIL: ny placement på team_b mangler';
   102	  end if;
   103	
   104	  -- ─── T3: _apply_employee_remove ──────────────────────────────────────
   105	  perform core_identity._apply_employee_remove(
   106	    jsonb_build_object('employee_id', v_emp_a_id::text, 'effective_from', (current_date + 1)::text),
   107	    null
   108	  );
   109	
   110	  if exists (
   111	    select 1 from core_identity.employee_node_placements
   112	    where employee_id = v_emp_a_id and effective_to is null
   113	  ) then
   114	    raise exception 'T3 FAIL: efter remove skal ingen open-ended placement findes for fixture-employee';
   115	  end if;
   116	
   117	  -- ─── T4: Authenticated direkte kald af _apply_*-handlers afvises ──────
   118	  -- Permission-denied rejection sker FØR handleren rør state; fixture-IDs
   119	  -- bruges som payload-input men handlerens revoke from authenticated
   120	  -- raiser 42501 inden noget INSERT/UPDATE.
   121	  begin
   122	    v_caught := null;
   123	    set local role authenticated;
   124	    perform core_identity._apply_employee_place(
   125	      jsonb_build_object('employee_id', v_emp_a_id::text, 'node_id', v_team_id::text, 'effective_from', current_date::text),
   126	      null
   127	    );
   128	    reset role;
   129	  exception when sqlstate '42501' then
   130	    v_caught := 'ok';
   131	    reset role;
   132	  end;
   133	  if v_caught is null then
   134	    raise exception 'T4 FAIL: authenticated kald skal afvises';
   135	  end if;
   136	
   137	  -- ─── T5: _apply_client_place → team-only validering ──────────────────
   138	  perform core_identity._apply_client_place(
   139	    jsonb_build_object('client_id', v_client_id::text, 'node_id', v_team_id::text, 'effective_from', current_date::text),
   140	    null
   141	  );
   142	
   143	  if not exists (
   144	    select 1 from core_identity.client_node_placements
   145	    where client_id = v_client_id and node_id = v_team_id and effective_to is null
   146	  ) then
   147	    raise exception 'T5 FAIL: client placement på team mangler';
   148	  end if;

   156	    );

   158	  if v_caught is null then
   159	    raise exception 'T6 FAIL: client placement på department skal blokeres af team-only trigger';
   160	  end if;
   161

   163	  -- Placér fixture-employee på team_a igen (efter T3's remove).
   164	  perform core_identity._apply_employee_place(
   165	    jsonb_build_object('employee_id', v_emp_a_id::text, 'node_id', v_team_id::text, 'effective_from', (current_date + 2)::text),
   166	    null
   167	  );

   171	    null
   172	  );

   178	  ) then

     2	--
     3	-- Minimal smoke — wrappers er tynde passthroughs til pending_change_request +
     4	-- apply-handlers (testet i Steps 1-5).
     5	--
     6	-- T0: Uden auth → permission_denied (PR #39 pattern: has_permission FØR validation)
     7	-- T1: Med superadmin auth → invalid node_type → 22023 (validation-path)
     8	-- T2: Med superadmin auth → client_node_place på department → 22023 (team-only pre-check)
     9	-- T3: Med superadmin auth → team_close på department → 22023 (node_type pre-check)
    10	--
    11	-- HERMETIC FIXTURE (G053 refactor 2026-05-19 / Mathias Vej D):
    12	-- Denne test bruger eksisterende superadmin read-only som auth-caller for at
    13	-- nå authorized wrapper-path. Den muterer IKKE seed-employees; alle business-
    14	-- fixtures er transaction-local throwaway rows (org_nodes, names, client uuids).
    15	-- Auth-caller-pattern bruger generisk superadmin-lookup, ikke hardcoded mg@/km@.
    16	
    17	begin;
    18

    21	  v_caught text;
    22	  v_dept_id uuid;
    23	  v_uuid_suffix text;
    24	  v_superadmin_auth_id uuid;
    25	begin
    26	  perform set_config('stork.source_type', 'manual', true);
    27	  perform set_config('stork.change_reason', 'T9 step 8 smoke hermetic fixture', true);
    28	
    29	  v_uuid_suffix := replace(gen_random_uuid()::text, '-', '');
    30	
    31	  -- Setup throwaway dept-knude (current_date - 10).
    32	  v_dept_id := gen_random_uuid();
    33	  insert into core_identity.org_nodes (id) values (v_dept_id);
    34	  insert into core_identity.org_node_versions
    35	    (node_id, name, parent_id, node_type, is_active, effective_from)
    36	  values
    37	    (v_dept_id, 'TestDept_' || v_uuid_suffix, null, 'department', true, current_date - 10);
    38

    40	  -- Ingen JWT claim sat → current_employee_id() er null → has_permission
    41	  -- returnerer false → wrapper raiser 42501 FØR validation.
    42	  begin
    43	    v_caught := null;
    44	    perform core_identity.org_node_upsert(null, 'unauth_' || v_uuid_suffix, null, 'invalid_type', true, current_date);
    45	  exception when sqlstate '42501' then v_caught := 'ok'; end;
    46	  if v_caught is null then
    47	    raise exception 'T0 FAIL: unauthenticated kald skal afvises med 42501 før validation';
    48	  end if;
    49	
    50	  -- ─── Authorized superadmin context ────────────────────────────────────
    51	  -- Find generisk superadmin med active auth_user_id. Setup-fail hvis ingen.
    52	  select e.auth_user_id into v_superadmin_auth_id
    53	  from core_identity.employees e
    54	  join core_identity.roles r on r.id = e.role_id
    55	  where r.name = 'superadmin'
    56	    and e.auth_user_id is not null
    57	    and core_identity.is_active_employee_state(e.anonymized_at, e.termination_date)

    62	  end if;
    63

    65	
    66	  -- Verificér at superadmin har de permissions wrapper-T1/T2/T3 kræver.
    67	  if not core_identity.has_permission('org_nodes', 'manage', true) then
    68	    raise exception 'SETUP FAIL: superadmin mangler org_nodes/manage/can_edit (M1-seed?)';
    69	  end if;
    70	  if not core_identity.has_permission('client_placements', 'manage', true) then
    71	    raise exception 'SETUP FAIL: superadmin mangler client_placements/manage/can_edit (M1-seed?)';
    72	  end if;

   153	-- der ændrer org_træ.
   154	--
   155	-- Dispatcher-mapping change_type → has_permission(page_key, can_edit=true):
   156	--   org_node_upsert     → 'org_nodes'           (struktur-ændring af knude)
   157	--   org_node_deactivate → 'org_nodes'           (struktur-ændring af knude)
   158	--   team_close          → 'org_nodes'           (lukker team-knude — struktur)
   159	--   employee_place      → 'employee_placements' (medarbejder-placering)
   160	--   employee_remove     → 'employee_placements' (medarbejder-placering)
   161	--   client_place        → 'client_placements'   (klient-placering)
   162	--   client_close        → 'client_placements'   (klient-placering)
   163	--
   164	-- Mappingen er system-mekanik (kode-logik), IKKE UI-styret data. Samme princip
   165	-- som apply-handlers' dispatcher per change_type. Mappingen er udtømmende;
   166	-- ukendt change_type raiser exception.
   167	--
   168	-- is_admin() self-approve-undtagelsen bevares: en admin kan approve sin egen
   169	-- request (§1.1's undtagelse for bootstrap-flows).
   170	create or replace function core_identity.pending_change_approve(
   171	  p_change_id uuid
   172	) returns void
   173	language plpgsql
   174	security invoker
   175	set search_path = ''
   176	as $$
   177	declare
   178	  v_change record;
   179	  v_approver uuid;
   180	  v_undo_period integer;
   181	  v_page_key text;
   182	begin
   183	  v_approver := core_identity.current_employee_id();
   184	  if v_approver is null then
   185	    raise exception 'no_authenticated_employee'
   186	      using errcode = '42501';
   187	  end if;
   188	
   189	  select * into v_change
   190	  from core_identity.pending_changes
   191	  where id = p_change_id
   192	  for update;
   193	
   194	  if not found then
   195	    raise exception 'pending_change_not_found %', p_change_id
   196	      using errcode = 'P0002';
   197	  end if;
   198	
   199	  if v_change.status <> 'pending' then
   200	    raise exception 'pending_change_wrong_status: % (expected pending)', v_change.status
   201	      using errcode = '22023';
   202	  end if;
   203	
   204	  -- Dispatcher: map change_type → underliggende ressource (page_key).
   205	  -- Approve af pending change kræver can_edit på samme page som ændringen rammer.
   206	  case v_change.change_type
   207	    when 'org_node_upsert'     then v_page_key := 'org_nodes';
   208	    when 'org_node_deactivate' then v_page_key := 'org_nodes';
   209	    when 'team_close'          then v_page_key := 'org_nodes';
   210	    when 'employee_place'      then v_page_key := 'employee_placements';
   211	    when 'employee_remove'     then v_page_key := 'employee_placements';
   212	    when 'client_place'        then v_page_key := 'client_placements';
   213	    when 'client_close'        then v_page_key := 'client_placements';
   214	    else
   215	      raise exception 'unknown_change_type for approve-gate: %', v_change.change_type
   216	        using errcode = '42883';
   217	  end case;
   218	
   219	  if not core_identity.has_permission(v_page_key, null, true) then
   220	    raise exception 'permission_denied: approve % kræver can_edit på %', v_change.change_type, v_page_key
   221	      using errcode = '42501';
   222	  end if;
   223	
   224	  if v_change.requested_by = v_approver and not core_identity.is_admin() then
   225	    raise exception 'pending_change_self_approve_forbidden'
   226	      using errcode = '42501', hint = 'requester må ikke selv approve (medmindre admin)';
   227	  end if;
   228	
   229	  select undo_period_seconds into v_undo_period
   230	  from core_identity.undo_settings
   231	  where change_type = v_change.change_type;
   232	
   233	  if v_undo_period is null then
   234	    v_undo_period := 24 * 3600;
   235	  end if;
   236	
   237	  perform set_config('stork.t9_write_authorized', 'true', true);
   238	  perform set_config('stork.source_type', 'manual', true);
   239	  perform set_config('stork.change_reason', 'pending_change_approve', true);
   240	
   241	  update core_identity.pending_changes
   242	  set status = 'approved',
   243	      approved_by = v_approver,
   244	      approved_at = now(),
   245	      undo_deadline = now() + (v_undo_period || ' seconds')::interval,
   246	      updated_at = now()
   247	  where id = p_change_id;
   248	end;
   249	$$;
   250	revoke execute on function core_identity.pending_change_approve(uuid) from public, anon;
   251	
   252	-- 2.2 pending_change_undo (Step 1, UPDATE pending_changes)
   253	--
   254	-- Undo af pending change kræver samme can_edit-rettighed på underliggende
   255	-- ressource som approve af samme change. Dispatcher-mapping identisk med
   256	-- pending_change_approve.
   257	create or replace function core_identity.pending_change_undo(
   258	  p_change_id uuid
   259	) returns void
   260	language plpgsql
   261	security invoker
   262	set search_path = ''
   263	as $$
   264	declare
   265	  v_change record;
   266	  v_page_key text;
   267	begin
   268	  select * into v_change
   269	  from core_identity.pending_changes
   270	  where id = p_change_id

 succeeded in 0ms:
   270	  where id = p_change_id
   271	  for update;
   272	
   273	  if not found then
   274	    raise exception 'pending_change_not_found %', p_change_id
   275	      using errcode = 'P0002';
   276	  end if;
   277	
   278	  if v_change.status <> 'approved' then
   279	    raise exception 'pending_change_wrong_status: % (expected approved)', v_change.status
   280	      using errcode = '22023';
   281	  end if;
   282	
   283	  if v_change.undo_deadline <= now() then
   284	    raise exception 'undo_deadline_expired'
   285	      using errcode = '22023',
   286	            hint = format('deadline var %s', v_change.undo_deadline);
   287	  end if;
   288	
   289	  -- Dispatcher: samme mapping som pending_change_approve.
   290	  case v_change.change_type
   291	    when 'org_node_upsert'     then v_page_key := 'org_nodes';
   292	    when 'org_node_deactivate' then v_page_key := 'org_nodes';
   293	    when 'team_close'          then v_page_key := 'org_nodes';
   294	    when 'employee_place'      then v_page_key := 'employee_placements';
   295	    when 'employee_remove'     then v_page_key := 'employee_placements';
   296	    when 'client_place'        then v_page_key := 'client_placements';
   297	    when 'client_close'        then v_page_key := 'client_placements';
   298	    else
   299	      raise exception 'unknown_change_type for undo-gate: %', v_change.change_type
   300	        using errcode = '42883';
   301	  end case;
   302	
   303	  if not core_identity.has_permission(v_page_key, null, true) then
   304	    raise exception 'permission_denied: undo % kræver can_edit på %', v_change.change_type, v_page_key
   305	      using errcode = '42501';
   306	  end if;
   307	
   308	  perform set_config('stork.t9_write_authorized', 'true', true);
   309	  perform set_config('stork.source_type', 'manual', true);
   310	  perform set_config('stork.change_reason', 'pending_change_undo', true);
   311	
   312	  update core_identity.pending_changes
   313	  set status = 'undone',
   314	      undone_at = now(),
   315	      updated_at = now()
   316	  where id = p_change_id;
   317	end;
   318	$$;
   319	revoke execute on function core_identity.pending_change_undo(uuid) from public, anon;

   322	create or replace function core_identity.undo_setting_update(
   323	  p_change_type text,
   324	  p_undo_period_seconds integer
   325	) returns void
   326	language plpgsql
   327	security invoker
   328	set search_path = ''
   329	as $$
   330	declare
   331	  v_updater uuid;
   332	begin
   333	  v_updater := core_identity.current_employee_id();
   334	  if v_updater is null then
   335	    raise exception 'no_authenticated_employee'
   336	      using errcode = '42501';
   337	  end if;
   338	
   339	  if not core_identity.has_permission('pending_changes', 'settings', true) then
   340	    raise exception 'permission_denied: pending_changes/settings/can_edit'
   341	      using errcode = '42501';
   342	  end if;
   343	
   344	  perform set_config('stork.t9_write_authorized', 'true', true);
   345	  perform set_config('stork.source_type', 'manual', true);
   346	  perform set_config('stork.change_reason', 'undo_setting_update', true);
   347

   349	  values (p_change_type, p_undo_period_seconds, now(), v_updater)

   351	  set undo_period_seconds = excluded.undo_period_seconds,
   352	      updated_at = excluded.updated_at,
   353	      updated_by = excluded.updated_by;
   354	end;
   355	$$;

/bin/bash -lc "nl -ba supabase/migrations/20260514120003_t1_audit_partitioned.sql | sed -n '86,164p'" in /home/mathias/stork-2.0
 succeeded in 0ms:
    86	-- source_type-detection-prioritet (§1.3):
    87	--  1. Session-var stork.source_type (eksplicit override)
    88	--  2. pg_trigger_depth() > 1 → trigger_cascade
    89	--  3. current_user IN ('service_role', 'supabase_admin') → service_role
    90	--  4. auth.uid() IS NOT NULL → manual
    91	--  5. fallback → unknown
    92	
    93	create or replace function core_compliance.stork_audit()
    94	returns trigger
    95	language plpgsql
    96	security definer
    97	set search_path = ''
    98	as $$
    99	declare
   100	  v_source_type text;
   101	  v_change_reason text;
   102	  v_old jsonb;
   103	  v_new jsonb;
   104	  v_changed text[];
   105	  v_record_id uuid;
   106	  v_actor uuid := auth.uid();
   107	begin
   108	  -- source_type detection
   109	  v_source_type := current_setting('stork.source_type', true);
   110	  if v_source_type is null or v_source_type = '' then
   111	    if pg_trigger_depth() > 1 then
   112	      v_source_type := 'trigger_cascade';
   113	    elsif current_user in ('service_role', 'supabase_admin') then
   114	      v_source_type := 'service_role';
   115	    elsif v_actor is not null then
   116	      v_source_type := 'manual';
   117	    else
   118	      v_source_type := 'unknown';
   119	    end if;
   120	  end if;
   121	
   122	  v_change_reason := current_setting('stork.change_reason', true);
   123	  if v_change_reason is null or length(trim(v_change_reason)) = 0 then
   124	    -- For cron og trigger_cascade kan change_reason mangle — kræv ellers.
   125	    if v_source_type in ('cron', 'trigger_cascade') then
   126	      v_change_reason := 'auto: ' || tg_op || ' on ' || tg_table_schema || '.' || tg_table_name;
   127	    else
   128	      raise exception 'stork.change_reason session-var er påkrævet for source_type=%', v_source_type
   129	        using errcode = 'P0001';
   130	    end if;
   131	  end if;
   132	
   133	  -- Bestem record_id (kræver id-kolonne af type uuid på target-tabel).
   134	  if tg_op = 'DELETE' then
   135	    v_record_id := (to_jsonb(old) ->> 'id')::uuid;
   136	    v_old := core_compliance.audit_filter_values(tg_table_schema, tg_table_name, to_jsonb(old));
   137	    v_new := null;
   138	  elsif tg_op = 'INSERT' then
   139	    v_record_id := (to_jsonb(new) ->> 'id')::uuid;
   140	    v_old := null;
   141	    v_new := core_compliance.audit_filter_values(tg_table_schema, tg_table_name, to_jsonb(new));
   142	  else  -- UPDATE
   143	    v_record_id := (to_jsonb(new) ->> 'id')::uuid;
   144	    v_old := core_compliance.audit_filter_values(tg_table_schema, tg_table_name, to_jsonb(old));
   145	    v_new := core_compliance.audit_filter_values(tg_table_schema, tg_table_name, to_jsonb(new));
   146	    -- changed_columns: kolonner hvor old != new
   147	    select array_agg(key)
   148	    into v_changed
   149	    from jsonb_each(to_jsonb(new)) n
   150	    where to_jsonb(old)->>n.key is distinct from n.value::text;
   151	  end if;
   152	
   153	  insert into core_compliance.audit_log (
   154	    occurred_at, table_schema, table_name, record_id, operation,
   155	    actor_user_id, actor_role, source_type, change_reason,
   156	    schema_version, changed_columns, old_values, new_values, trigger_depth
   157	  ) values (
   158	    now(), tg_table_schema, tg_table_name, v_record_id, tg_op,
   159	    v_actor, current_user, v_source_type, v_change_reason,
   160	    1, v_changed, v_old, v_new, pg_trigger_depth()
   161	  );
   162	
   163	  return null;  -- AFTER-trigger
   164	end;

KRITISK-SIKKERHEDSHUL: T10.4 klassificerer `core_identity.clients.logo_filename` som `pii_level='none'`.

Write-flow: T10.11 `client_logo_set` skriver brugerleveret `p_logo_filename` til `clients.logo_filename`. `clients_audit` kalder `audit_filter_values`, og T10.4’s klassifikation betyder at filnavnet lander i `audit_log` i klartekst. Det er inkonsistent med at `clients.name` klassificeres som direct PII, fordi originalt filnavn realistisk kan indeholde klient-/personidentifikatorer.

LØS: Skift T10.4-klassifikation for `clients.logo_filename` til `pii_level='direct'`, så eksisterende audit-filter hasher feltet. Udvid `t10_client_logo.sql` med assertion for at `logo_filename` hashes i audit ved `client_logo_set` / `client_logo_clear`.

STOP — Runde 11 afventer LØS-svar.

codex
TEKNISK-BLOKERING: T10.15 `t10_client_active_check.sql` kan ikke verificere apply-path som skrevet.

Fund: Testplanen siger flere steder “approve+apply” direkte efter `client_node_place` pending-oprettelse. Men eksisterende T9 seed sætter `undo_settings` for `client_place`/`client_close` til `24 * 3600`, og `pending_change_apply` stopper med `not_yet_due` før dispatch til `_apply_client_place`.

Konsekvens: T10.15 T1/T3/T6/T7/T8 tester ikke klient-aktiv-checken i apply-handleren; de rammer due-gate før den nye T10.7b-logik. Det bryder eksempel-row-gennem-flow for write-vejen.

LØS: Specificér i T10.15 setup at testen enten:
- sætter `undo_settings.undo_period_seconds = 0` for `client_place`/`client_close` transaction-local, eller
- opdaterer den konkrete `pending_changes.undo_deadline <= now()` med `stork.t9_write_authorized='true'` før `pending_change_apply`.

Derefter skal assertions forvente `_apply_client_place`-resultatet, ikke due-gate-resultatet.
tokens used
178,099
TEKNISK-BLOKERING: T10.15 `t10_client_active_check.sql` kan ikke verificere apply-path som skrevet.

Fund: Testplanen siger flere steder “approve+apply” direkte efter `client_node_place` pending-oprettelse. Men eksisterende T9 seed sætter `undo_settings` for `client_place`/`client_close` til `24 * 3600`, og `pending_change_apply` stopper med `not_yet_due` før dispatch til `_apply_client_place`.

Konsekvens: T10.15 T1/T3/T6/T7/T8 tester ikke klient-aktiv-checken i apply-handleren; de rammer due-gate før den nye T10.7b-logik. Det bryder eksempel-row-gennem-flow for write-vejen.

LØS: Specificér i T10.15 setup at testen enten:
- sætter `undo_settings.undo_period_seconds = 0` for `client_place`/`client_close` transaction-local, eller
- opdaterer den konkrete `pending_changes.undo_deadline <= now()` med `stork.t9_write_authorized='true'` før `pending_change_apply`.

Derefter skal assertions forvente `_apply_client_place`-resultatet, ikke due-gate-resultatet.

  1003	async function postgrestT9SchemaExposure() {
  1004	  const token = process.env.SUPABASE_ACCESS_TOKEN;
  1005	  const projectRef = process.env.SUPABASE_PROJECT_REF || "imtxvrymaqbgcvsarlib";
  1006	
  1007	  // T9-supplement Step 5 + Codex runde 2 follow-up: deterministisk schema-exposure-
  1008	  // canary via PostgREST OpenAPI-introspection (ikke RPC-call). Service_role har
  1009	  // ingen direkte data-grants på core_identity-tabeller — en security-invoker RPC
  1010	  // ville fejle med 42501 uanset om schemaet er korrekt eksponeret. OpenAPI-spec
  1011	  // verificerer schema + cache-state uden at kræve tabel-access.
  1012	  // Hard-fail hvis SUPABASE_ACCESS_TOKEN mangler i CI; skip lokalt for udvikler-flow.
  1013	  if (!token) {
  1014	    return {
  1015	      name: "postgrest-t9-schema-exposure",
  1016	      violations: [],
  1017	      skipped: "SUPABASE_ACCESS_TOKEN ikke sat (lokal udvikler-mode)",
  1018	    };
  1019	  }
  1020	
  1021	  let serviceRoleKey;
  1022	  try {
  1023	    const apiKeysRes = await fetch(`https://api.supabase.com/v1/projects/${projectRef}/api-keys`, {
  1024	      headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${token}` },
  1025	    });
  1026	    if (!apiKeysRes.ok) {
  1027	      return {
  1028	        name: "postgrest-t9-schema-exposure",
  1029	        violations: [`Management API /api-keys returned ${apiKeysRes.status}`],
  1030	      };
  1031	    }
  1032	    const keys = await apiKeysRes.json();
  1033	    const serviceKeyEntry = (Array.isArray(keys) ? keys : keys.data || []).find(
  1034	      (k) => k.name === "service_role" || k.type === "service_role",
  1035	    );
  1036	    if (!serviceKeyEntry) {
  1037	      return {
  1038	        name: "postgrest-t9-schema-exposure",
  1039	        violations: [`service_role-key ikke fundet i /api-keys response`],
  1040	      };
  1041	    }
  1042	    serviceRoleKey = serviceKeyEntry.api_key;
  1043	  } catch (err) {
  1044	    return {
  1045	      name: "postgrest-t9-schema-exposure",
  1046	      violations: [`Netværksfejl ved api-keys-hent: ${err.message}`],
  1047	    };
  1048	  }
  1049	
  1050	  // PostgREST OpenAPI-introspection: GET /rest/v1/ med Accept-Profile=core_identity.
  1051	  // Hvis schemaet er eksponeret + cachen er fresh, returnerer PostgREST en OpenAPI
  1052	  // spec hvor T9-RPCs (org_tree_read etc.) er listet under "paths". Verifikationen
  1053	  // kræver ingen tabel-SELECT-grant på service_role (modsat tidligere RPC-call —
  1054	  // service_role har bevidst ingen direkte data-grants på core_identity, så et
  1055	  // RPC-call med security invoker ville fejle med 42501 selv ved korrekt exposure).
  1056	  //
  1057	  // Sentinel-RPCs der skal være i spec'en for at bevise schema + cache er friske.
  1058	  const expectedRpcs = [
  1059	    "/rpc/org_tree_read",
  1060	    "/rpc/permission_elements_read",
  1061	    "/rpc/employee_placement_read",
  1062	    "/rpc/client_placement_read",
  1063	    "/rpc/pending_changes_read",
  1064	  ];
  1065	
  1066	  try {
  1067	    const specRes = await fetch(`https://${projectRef}.supabase.co/rest/v1/`, {
  1068	      method: "GET",
  1069	      headers: {
  1070	        apikey: serviceRoleKey,
  1071	        Authorization: `Bearer ${serviceRoleKey}`,
  1072	        "Accept-Profile": "core_identity",
  1073	        Accept: "application/openapi+json",
  1074	      },
  1075	    });
  1076	
  1077	    if (!specRes.ok) {
  1078	      const body = await specRes.text();
  1079	      return {
  1080	        name: "postgrest-t9-schema-exposure",
  1081	        violations: [
  1082	          `OpenAPI-introspection fejlede: HTTP ${specRes.status}. ` +
  1083	            `Forventet 200 med Accept-Profile: core_identity. ` +
  1084	            `Body: ${body.slice(0, 200)}`,
  1085	        ],
  1086	      };
  1087	    }
  1088	
  1089	    const spec = await specRes.json();
  1090	    const paths = (spec && spec.paths) || {};
  1091	    const missing = expectedRpcs.filter((p) => !(p in paths));
  1092	    if (missing.length > 0) {
  1093	      return {
  1094	        name: "postgrest-t9-schema-exposure",
  1095	        violations: [
  1096	          `core_identity er eksponeret men T9-RPCs mangler i OpenAPI-spec: ${missing.join(", ")}. ` +
  1097	            `Mulige årsager: PostgREST schema-cache stale (notify pgrst, 'reload schema'), ` +
  1098	            `eller RPC'erne mangler i remote DB (tjek migrations-state).`,
  1099	        ],
  1100	      };
  1101	    }
  1102	    return { name: "postgrest-t9-schema-exposure", violations: [] };
  1103	  } catch (err) {
  1104	    return {
  1105	      name: "postgrest-t9-schema-exposure",
  1106	      violations: [`Netværksfejl ved OpenAPI-introspection: ${err.message}`],
  1107	    };
  1108	  }
  1109	}
  1110

  1116	    entries = await readdir(join(ROOT, dir), { withFileTypes: true });
  1117	  } catch {
  1118	    return { name: "db-test-no-t9-skip-guards", violations };
  1119	  }
  1120	  // Skip-guard-mønster: information_schema.tables-lookup + raise notice "skipping" + early return.

     3	-- Master-plan §1.2: hver kolonne i hele systemet har eksplicit semantik.

     8	
     9	create table core_compliance.data_field_definitions (
    10	  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
    11	  table_schema text not null,
    12	  table_name text not null,
    13	  column_name text not null,
    14	  category text not null check (category in (
    15	    'operationel', 'konfiguration', 'master_data', 'audit', 'raw_payload'
    16	  )),
    17	  pii_level text not null check (pii_level in ('none', 'indirect', 'direct')),
    18	  retention_type text check (retention_type in ('time_based', 'event_based', 'legal', 'manual')),
    19	  retention_value jsonb,
    20	  match_role text,
    21	  purpose text not null check (length(trim(purpose)) > 0),
    22	  created_at timestamptz not null default now(),
    23	  updated_at timestamptz not null default now(),
    24	  -- Retention-konsistens: type+value følges ad eller begge NULL
    25	  constraint retention_consistency check (
    26	    (retention_type is null and retention_value is null)
    27	    or (retention_type is not null and retention_value is not null)
    28	  ),
    29	  unique (table_schema, table_name, column_name)
    30	);
